vyāsa kṛtam yasya ājñayā jagatsraṣṭā virañciḥ pālakaḥ hāraḥ tīrthānām uttamam tīrtha kṣetrāṇām kṣetram uttamam munīnām āśrayaḥ nityam naimiṣa araṇyam uttamam śaunaka ādyāḥ mahātmānaḥ śiva bhaktāḥ mahā ojasaḥ tasmin satre mahābhāgaḥ munīnām bhāgya gauravāt ājagāma munīn draṣṭum sūtaḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā te mahātmānaḥ naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ praśum udyuktāḥ papracchuḥ romaharṣaṇam ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ katham bhagavatā pūrvam ādityena ātma rūpiṇā purāṇam kathitam sauram tat naḥ vaktum iha arhasi kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt sākṣāt pūrve hi viditam tvayā tvattaḥ nā asti paraḥ vaktā purāṇānām mahā tapaḥ santi anye bahavaḥ śiṣyāḥ api tasya mahātmanaḥ tathā api īi śiṣya vātsalyāt tvam purāṇeṣu yojitaḥ yāni anyāni purāṇāni tvayā uktāni mahā mune śiva bhaktim ṛte yasmāt muktiḥ na asti iti śuśruma devaḥ ayam bhagavān bhānuḥ antaryāmī sanātanaḥ yaḥ brūte sarva vastūnām tattvam jñātvā eva na anyathā atas śraddhā hi mahatī śrotum tvad vadana amṛtam asmākam vartate sūtam romaharṣaṇa suvrata sūtaḥ uvāca natvā sūrya param dhāma ṛk yajuḥ sāma rūpiṇam purāṇam saṃpravakṣyāmi sauram śiva kathā āśrayam yat śrutvā manujaḥ śīghram pāpa kañcukam utsṛjet paurāṇī vṛttim āśritya ye jīvanti dvijātayaḥ māhātmyam kathyate śaṃbhar na asti asmāt adhikam dvijāḥ idam purāṇam vaktavyam dhārmikāya anasūyave dhānāya śiva eka atibuddhaye āsīt manuḥ sūrya sutaḥ vartate yaḥ mahā tapāḥ sa kadācid mahābhāgaḥ kāmika ākhyam vanam yayau tattvam vicārayāmāsuḥ mithas yatra mahā ṛṣayaḥ aśaktāḥ te mahābhāgāḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ tattva nirṇaye evam sthiteṣu vipreṣu māyayā mohita ātmasu saṃśaya āviṣṭa citteṣu vāc abhūt aśarīriṇī śrutvā tu munayaḥ sarve bhṛgu ādyāḥ dagdha kilviṣāḥ mā enum puraskṛtya yayuḥ kṣetram vai dvādaśa ātmanaḥ viśrutam dvādaśādityam iti lokeṣu tat vijāḥ paśyantu mām param devam viśva antaryāmiṇam vibhum sūtaḥ uvāca iti dṛṣṭvā ravim sākṣāt pratyakṣam puratas sthitam mene kṛtārtham ātmānam manuḥ vaivasvataḥ tadā ātmani ātmānam ādhāya sarva bhāvena saṃyamī nama namaḥ vareṇyāya vara dāya aṃśumāline tri loka cakṣuṣe tubhyam triguṇāya amṛtāya ca nara nārī śarīrāya namaḥ te ma jñānāya akhila īśāya sapta aśvāya trimūrtaye namaḥ vyāhṛti rūpāya tri lakṣāya āśu gāmine eka lakṣa vilakṣāya bahu lakṣāya daṇḍine eka saṃsthā dvi saṃsthāya bahu saṃsthāya te namaḥ śakti trayāya śuklāya ravaye parameṣṭhine tvam hariḥ deva tvam brahmā tvam divaspatiḥ tvam akāraḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ svadhā svāhā tvam eva hi tvām ṛte paramātmānam na tat paśyāmi daivatam munibhiḥ saha dharma ātmā samyak darśana kāṅkṣibhiḥ jñāte tasmin tu kim rūpam tasya jñānam kimātmakam caritam tasya kim tāta kim tīrtham tad adhiṣṭhitam lakṣaṇam ca purāṇānām vratānām ca kramaḥ yathā varṇānām āśramāṇām ca varṇa ācāra vidhiḥ katham śrāddham katham vā kriyate prāyaścitta vidhiḥ katham etat sarvam hi bhagavan pṛṣṭam vaktum iha arhasi evam manoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhāskaraḥ dvijāḥ yat pṛṣṭam tat aśeṣeṇa vaktum samupacakrame iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde naimiṣāraṇyapraśaṃsādikathanam nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi tattvam yatra pratiṣṭhitam purāṇe asmin mahābhāga sarva veda artha saṃgrahe tattvam yat bhagavataḥ rūpam īśasya śūlinaḥ viśvam tena akhilam vyāptam na anyena iti abravīt śrutiḥ saḥ eva ātmā samastānām bhūtānām manuja adhipa caitanya rūpī bhagavān mahādevaḥ saha umayā bahudhā bhāti līlayā kevalaḥ śivaḥ brahma viṣṇu ādi rūpeṇa devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ pṛṣṭaḥ brahma ādibhiḥ devaiḥ kaḥ tvam deva iti śaṃkaraḥ abravīt aham eva ekaḥ na anyaḥ kaścid iti śrutiḥ ātma bhūtān mahādevān līlā vigraha rūpiṇaḥ tam ekam paramātmānam ādi kartāram īśvaram prāhuḥ bahuvidham tad jñāḥ indram mitram iti śrutiḥ na tasmāt adhikaḥ kaścid na aṇīyān api kaścana tena idam akhilam pūrṇa śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā mumukṣubhiḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ śivaḥ ekaḥ nirañjanaḥ ānanda rūpayā gauryā krīḍati sma maheśvaraḥ akṣeram paramam vyoma śaivam jyotiḥ anāmayam na anyaḥ vedyaḥ svayam jyotīḥ rudraḥ ekaḥ nirañjanaḥ tasmin jñāte akhilam jñātam iti āhuḥ veda vādinaḥ aham brahmā ca śakraḥ ca anye divaukasaḥ adya api upāyaiḥ vividhaiḥ śaṃbhoḥ darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ bhaktyā eva ananyayā rājan jñāyate bhagavān aśivaḥ bhargāt viśvasya bharaṇāt viśvayoneḥ umāpateḥ tasya jñāna mayī śaktiḥ avyayā girijā śivā ācakṣate tayoḥ bhedam ajñāḥ na paramārthataḥ māyā sā paramā śaktiḥ akṣa erā girijā avyayā māyā viśva ātmakaḥ rudra rata jñātvā hi amṛtī bhavet dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām prāyaṇe kāraṇam param śiva bhaktiḥ sadā satyam na anya kiṃcana bhū tale trilokyām sukha kāmaḥ yaḥ tena pūjyaḥ sadāśivaḥ śiva bhaktiḥ mṛte saukhyam kutas syāt dehinām śiva bhaktyā dhanam vidyā yaśaḥ yadā lalāṭe sukha prāptiḥ likhitā bhavet sadā śiva sevāyām matiḥ bhavati iti veda siddhāntaḥ sva ātmani avasthitam devam viśva vyāpinam īśvaram bhaktyā paramayā rājan jñātvā pāśaiḥ vimucyate saṃkalam tasya bhāsā eva bhāti na anyena śaṃkaraḥ tasmin prakāśamāne hi nā eva bhānti anala ādayaḥ tasmin maheśvare gūḍhe vidyā avidye kṣara akṣare vidhātari jagannāthe viśvam bhāti na vastutas tasmin jñāte akhilaiḥ pāśaiḥ mucyate manuja īśvaraḥ sarve krīḍanakāḥ tasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ ādisarge mahādevaḥ brahmāṇam asṛjat prabhuḥ dakṣiṇa aṅgāt virūpākṣaḥ sṛṣṭi arthe līlayā kila asṛjat pālana artham ca vāma bhāgāt maheśvaraḥ hṛdayāt kāla rudra ākhyam jaga saṃhāra kārakam asṛjat yoginām dhyeyaḥ nirguṇaḥ tu svayam śivaḥ viśvam tasmāt hi saṃbhūtam tasmin tiṣṭhati śaṃkare saḥ eva ātmā mahādevaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām bhakti yuktena jñātavyaḥ parameśvaraḥ na paśyāmi mahādevāt adhikam devatā antaram vedāḥ api tam eva artham āhuḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare vedāḥ ūcuḥ yam prapaśyanti vidvāṃsaḥ yoginaḥ kṣapita āśayāḥ niyamya karaṇa grāmam saḥ eva ātmā maheśvaraḥ yasya prasādāt jīvanti sa devaḥ pārvatīpatiḥ na jānanti param bhāvam yasya brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ śṛṇvantu devatāḥ sarvāḥ satyam asmad vacaḥ param na asti rudrāt mahādevāt adhikam daivatam param na yathā kūrma romāṇi śṛṅgam na śaśa mastake mahādevam vijānīyāt deham asmi iti paṇḍitaḥ brāhmī nārāyaṇī raudrī pū̃jayitvā maheśvarīm yat prapaśyanti yogi indrāt tat vidyāt śāṃkaram padam kramāt catrāṇi caṃkramya śaṅkhinyām upari sthitam deva yāna patham hitvā pitṛyāṇam tathā uttaram gagana ādyaḥ ravaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śaṃkarasya sa vācakaḥ viśvatas cakṣuḥ īśāna triśūlī viśvatomukhaḥ janakaḥ sarva bhūtānām ekaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ vāla agra mātram hṛd padme sthitam devam umāpatim ye anupaśyanti teṣām śāntiḥ hi śāśvatī pṛthivyām tiṣṭhati vibhuḥ pṛthivī vetti nā eva tam rūpam ca pṛthivī yasya tasmai bhūmi ātmane namaḥ yosar tiṣṭhati ameya ātmā na tam vetti kadācana sūrye tiṣṭhati yaḥ devaḥ na sūryaḥ vetti śaṃkaram yaḥ candre tiṣṭhati virbhuḥ candraḥ vetti na śāśvatam yajamānaḥ api yat rūpam yajamāna ātmane namaḥ pramāṇa padam ārūḍhāḥ tvad prasādāt vṛṣadhvaja bhānuḥ uvāca evam veda stutim śrutvā bhagavān girijāpatiḥ pratyakṣaḥ samabhūt teṣām vedānām manuja adhipa sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ sūrya soma agni locanaḥ sthūlāt sthūlataraḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataraḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca mad prasādāt bhaviṣyadhvam he vedāḥ loka pūjitāḥ yuṣmān āśritya vipra indrāḥ karma kurvanti na anyathā niṣphalam tat bhavet karma teṣām yuṣmad daivajñayā nityam naimittikam kāmyam yat ca anyat mokṣa sādhanam ye vai yuṣmān an ādṛtya śāstram kurvanti mānavāḥ yuṣmad kṛtam param stotram ye paṭhiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ teṣām adhyayanam puṇyam mad prasādāt bhaviṣyati bhānuḥ uvāca akṣaram nirguṇam śuddham ānandam param avyayam pratyakṣam sarva bhūtānām ajñānām tad viparyayaḥ viśva māyā vidhātāram diḥ aṣṭādaśa rūpaṇam bhakti grādyam mahādevam jānīya ātmani saṃsthitam bhaktim āsthāya parama om param nirvāṇam āpnuhi tīrtha yātrāḥ bahuvidhāḥ yajñāḥ ca vividhāḥ kṛtāḥ yeṣām janma sahasreṣu teṣām bhaktiḥ bhavet śive tatra akṣayaḥ paraḥ dharmaḥ śiva dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ yajñāt tīrthāt japa ādānāt dharmaḥ syāt bahu sādhanaḥ sādhana prārthanā kleśaḥ para saṃpatti duḥkha daḥ saṃcitam janma sāhasraiḥ pāpam yadi te vijñeyāḥ mahātmānaḥ iti satyam bravīmi aham pādma kalpa samudbhūtām brahmaṇā samudīritām aśraddhayā parayā rājan śṛṇu tvam gadataḥ mama vakṣye aham tam bhuvana nāyakam āsīt ādye kṛta yuge sapta dvīpā eka rāvalī pratiṣṭhāna pure ramye gaṅgā tīre manorame tatra sthitvā akhilām pṛthvīm tasmin rājani śāsati kadācid tatra bhagavān tṛṇabinduḥ mahā muniḥ ājagāma sa tam su dyumnam priya darśanam tam āyāntam munim dṛṣṭvā rājā rudra arcane rataḥ udvāsya āca mahā bāhuḥ utthāya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ bhagavān āgataḥ yasmāt mām draṣṭum muni sattama bhānuḥ uvāca sudyumnasya vacaḥ śrutvā muniḥ āha mahā manāḥ tṛṇabinduḥ uvāca tathā api caritam śrutvā tava aham vismaya anvitaḥ kathayasva mahā bāho śrotum kautūhalam hi me jānāti bhagavān ekaḥ viśva vyāpī maheśvaraḥ idam puṇyam iti jñātvā kṛtam na anena yadi api āhara prahara ityādi nāma saṃkīrtanam ca yat karoti tena puṇyena duṣkṛtam bhasmasātkṛtam pāpa leśaḥ api na asya asti iti me niścitā matiḥ suvyāḍim pūjayāmāsa yathāvat vidhi pūrvakam sūryāta pratīkāśam divya strībhiḥ virājitam deva dūtaiḥ samānītam āruhya muni puṃgava tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān yugānām ayutam tatas tatas tu karmaṇaḥ śeṣam bhoktum atra mahī tale smarāmi pūrvikām jātim prasādāt śūlinaḥ mune jānāti kaḥ maheśasya māhātmyam paramātmanaḥ yasya nāmnaḥ phalam idam ajñāna uccāraṇāt api jñātvā yaḥ kīrtayet śam bhoḥ nāmāni amita tejasaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca iti sarvam aśeṣeṇa caritam tasya dhīmataḥ sunasya muniḥ śrutvā vismitaḥ abhūt punar punar mahātmānam sunam rāja puṃgavam rāja svam āśrama padam yāmi iti uktvā jagāma saḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure bhānu manu saṃvāde sudyunnākhyānam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ rājñaḥ sakāśāt sa muniḥ matvā kim kṛtavān punar bhānuḥ uvāca revā tīre mahat puṇyam jāleśvaram iti smṛtam āśramam tṛṇavindaḥ tu muni siddha niṣevitam śiva liṅga pratiṣṭhāpya tīrtha yātrām cakāra saḥ kāni tīrthāni guhyāni yeṣu saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca tīrthānām uttamam tīrtham kṣetrāṇām kṣetram uttamam vārāṇasī iti nagarī priyā devasya yaṃtra viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ sarveṣām iha dehinām dadāti tārakam jñānam saṃsārāt mocakam param gaṅgā brahma mayī yatra mūrtiḥ ca uttara bāhinī sarva pāpānām dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā namaskṛtā na asti gaṅgā samam tīrthe vārāṇasyām viśeṣataḥ kim tat śreyaskaram iti hṛdi kṛtvā jagāma saḥ nandīśvarasya yaḥ śiṣyaḥ yoginām agraṇīḥ svayam jānā deva gaṇa ākīrṇe yakṣa gandharva sevite siddha cāraṇa kūṣmāṇḍaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca saṃkule gaṅgā mandākinī yatra rājate duḥkha hāriṇī tasya āśramam anuprāpya pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ abhivādya yathānyāyam tasya agre upaviśya ca kṛta añjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā vākyam etat uvāca ha vyāsaḥ uvāca prāptam kali yugam ghoram puṇya mārga bahiṣkṛtam pākhaṇḍa ācāra niratam mleccha antra jana saṃkulam adhārmikāḥ krūraiḥ sattvāḥ dhanācīra alpa medhasaḥ tasmin yuge bhaviṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ śūdra yājakāḥ snānam deva arcanam dānam homam ca pitṛ tarpaṇam svādhyāyam na kariṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ hi kalau yuge na paṭhanti tathā vedān śreyase brāhmaṇa adhamāḥ pratigraha artham vedān ca paṭhiṣyanti kalau yuge puruṣottamam āśritya śiva nindā ratāḥ dvijāḥ kalau yuge bhaviṣyanti teṣām trātā na mādhavaḥ svām svām vṛttim parityajya para vṛtti upajīvakāḥ brāhmaṇa ādyāḥ bhaviṣyanti saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge etān pāpa ratān dṛṣṭvā rājānaḥ aśva avicārakāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte vṛthā jāti abhimāninaḥ ucca āsana gatāḥ śūdrāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca brāhmaṇān tadā kāṣāyaṇaḥ ca nirgranthāḥ nagnāḥ kāpālikāḥ tathā tapaḥ yajña phalānām tu vikretāraḥ dvija adhamāḥ yatayaḥ ca bhaviṣyanti śataśas atha sahasraśas vinindanti mahādevam saṃsārāt mocakam param tad bhaktān ca mahātmanaḥ brāhmaṇān ca kalau yuge tāḍayanti durātmānaḥ brāhmaṇān rāja sevakāḥ na nivārayate rājā tān dṛṣṭvā api kalau yuge iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure bhānu manu saṃbāde vārāṇasī mahimakaliyugavarṇanam nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ gaccha vārāṇasīm vyāsa yatra viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ viśveśvarasya yat liṅgam jyotirliṃṅgam tat ucyate yasmin dṛṣṭe kṣaṇāt jantuḥ saṃsāram na punar viśet gatvā paiśya param liṅgam tatra satyavatī suta snātvā gaṅgā jale puṇye paśya viśveśvaram param sa dāsyati param jñānam yena muktaḥ bhaviṣyasi dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaram devam yāvat tiṣṭhati tad kṣaṇāt āgamiṣyanti munayaḥ tvām draṣṭum sarve eva te brūhi mad vacanāt teṣām jñānam māheśvaram param evam satyavatī sūnuḥ tat māhātmyam aśeṣatas sanatkumārāt sva guroḥ śrutvā māheśvara agraṇīḥ sa śiṣyaḥ prayayau śīghram vyāsaḥ vārāṇasīm prati gatvā vārāṇasīm vyāsaḥ siddha ṛṣi muni sevitām bhānuḥ uvāca saṃprāpya kāśīm dharma ātmā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ snātvā yathāvat jāhnavyām tarpayitvā surān yayau viśveśvaram draṣṭum jyotiḥ liṅgat manāmayam saṃpūjya sarva bhāvena daṇḍa vat praṇipatya ca devasya dakṣiṇā mūrtau upaviśya mahā muniḥ paśyan viśveśvaram liṅgam jaipan vai śatarudriyam kṣaṇāt liṅgāt param jyotiḥ āvirbhūtam nirañjanam sūkṣmāt sūkṣmam ca paramam ānandam tamasaḥ param yat tat māheśvaram jyotiḥ vedānteṣu pratiṣṭhitam darśanāt tasya ca muneḥ pārāśaryasya dhīmataḥ divyam māheśvaram jñānam udbhūtam kevalam śivam advayam nirguṇam śāntam jīvanmuktaḥ tadā muniḥ yasmin dṛṣṭe kṣaṇāt jñānam uditam mama nirmalam namaḥ bhagavate tubhyam viśvanāthāya śūline durvijñeya aprameyāya paramānanda rūpiṇe bhakti priyāya sūkṣmāya pārvatīśāya te namaḥ jānāti viśveśa tattvataḥ mādṛśaḥ janaḥ vedāḥ api na jānanti sa aṅga upaniṣada kramāḥ bhānuḥ uvāca śūlapāṇiḥ ameya ātmā prādurāsīt vṛṣadhvajaḥ tatas tam abravīt vākyam kāruṇyāt śubhayā girā vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavan kṛtakṛtyaḥ asmi darśanāt tava śaṃkara jātam tvad viṣayam jñānam devānām api durlabham dehi me devadeveśa na anyat iṣṭam varam mama bhānuḥ uvāca varam dattvā muni indrāya kṣaṇāt antarhitaḥ abhavat tasmāt ṭhyāsāt paraḥ nā anyaḥ śiva bhaktaḥ jagāye kṛṣṇaḥ vā devakī sūnuḥ arjunaḥ vā mahāmatiḥ evam harāt labdha varaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ taṃtra yāni ca liṅgāni tāni draṣṭum yayau muniḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure bhānuka anusaṃvāde mahādeva varadānam nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kāni divyāni liṅgāni yāni draṣṭum yayau muniḥ ācakṣva tāni naḥ sūta māhātmyam ca api kṛtsnaśas sūtaḥ uvāca yat uktam bhānunā pūrva manave muni sattamāḥ tat eva kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama āgneyyām avimuktasya vāpī trailokya viśrutā yatra saṃnihitāḥ davaḥ nityam viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ yaṃtra snānam dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ devānām api durlabham teṣām liṅgāni jāyante hṛdaye trīṇi suvratāḥ tatra satyavatī sūnuḥ khātvā ca eva yathāvidhi avimukteśvaram dṛṣṭvā lāṅgalīśam tatas yayau tatra brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ sevante śūlapāṇinam tasya darśana mātreṇa jñānam pāśupatam bhavet jagāma sa muniḥ paśvā ādraṣṭum vai tārakeśvaram yatra anta kāle bhagavān jñānam tat saṃprayacchati tat dṛṣṭvā paramam liṅgam vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ yayau śukreśvaram draṣṭum sarva siddhi pradāyakam ārādhya muninā yatra śukreṇa amita tejasā prāptā saṃjīvanī vidyā surāṇām api durlabhā tasmin kūpe muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā śukreśvaram śivam brahmeśvaram yayau draṣṭum tatra brahmā virāj svayam tapaḥ taptvā mahā ghoram prītaye pārvatīpateḥ brahmatvam prāptavān brahmā yogam ca anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ yatra sākṣāt śivaḥ sūkṣmaḥ nityam tiṣṭhati vai dvijāḥ anugrahāya lokānām paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ yatra pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ oṃkāra īśvaram īśvaram saṃpūjya paramām siddhim prāsavantaḥ dvijottamāḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśyām tasmin liṅaḥ upoṣitaḥ yadi jāgaraṇam kuryāt param siddhim avāpnuyāt tatas satyavatī sūnuḥ kṛttivāsa īśvaram yayau upāsate mahādevam yatra brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ munayaḥ śaṃsita ātmānaḥ rudra jāpya parāyaṇāḥ kṛttivāseśvare bahavaḥ dvijāḥ snātvā tatra mahādevam kṛttivāsa īśvaram śivam sakṛt paśyati yaḥ bhaktyā kṛttivāsa īśvaram vibhum haṃsatīrthe naraḥ snātvā kṛttivāseśvaram vibhum saṃpūjya parayā bhaktyā kṛttivāsa īśvaram śivam na patati eva saṃsāre na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yayau ratneśvaram draṣṭum mokṣaḥ yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ yaḥ ayam pāśupataḥ yogaḥ paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ varṣeḥ dvādaśabhiḥ samyak kṛte pāśupate dvijāḥ ratneśvaram tu saṃpūjya pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ draṣṭum deva adhideveśam vṛddhakāleśvaram yayau tasmīt liṅga mahādevaḥ sadā tiṣṭhati līlayā anugrahāya lokānām ayā saha viśvabhuj pṛthivyām yāni liṅgāni santi divyāni vai dvijāḥ vṛddhakāleśvare dṛṣṭe dṛṣṭāni eva na saṃśayaḥ devasya pūrva digbhāge kūpa om muni niṣevitaḥ pūritaḥ puṇya salilaiḥ devadevena śaṃbhunā yaiḥ pītam tasya salilam prākṛtaiḥ culuka trayam tatra dvaipāyanaḥ viprāḥ snānam kṛtvā samāhitaḥ buddhakāleśvara liṅgam saṃpūjya ca tatas yayau madhyameśvara nāmānam mokṣa liṅgam anuttamam upāsate param liṅgam śiva darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ mandākinyām muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai madhyameśvaram ghaṇṭākarṇa snātvā liṅga tat vimalam śivam pratiṣṭhāpya muni śreṣṭhaḥ labdhavān jñānam uttamam dṛṣṭvā vyāseśvaram śivam yatra yatra mṛtaḥ vā api vārāṇasyām mṛtaḥ bhavet tatas satyavatī sūnuḥ kapardī īśvaram īśvaram draṣṭum jagāma dipa indrāḥ liṅgam tat pārameśvaram ye drakṣyanti kapardīśam kṛtārthāḥ te na saṃśayaḥ mānuṣīm tanum āśritya rudrāḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ tasmin tīrthe muniḥ snātvā saṃtarpya ca surān pitṝn kapardīśvaram īśānam saṃpūjya prayayau muniḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde vārāṇasī liṅga pahimavarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca punar jagāma bhagavān kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ dakṣeśvaram devam bhaktānām siddhi dāyakam yat śiva avajñayā pāpam jātam dakṣa prajāpateḥ tasya pāpasya mokṣāya tasmāt liṅge dvijottamāḥ ārādhya devadeveśam bahūni abda śatāni vai vairam nidhāya manasi śaṃbhunā saha suvratāḥ dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ yajñam akarot jāhnavī taṭe tasmin yajñe samāhūtāḥ indra ādyāḥ devatā gaṇāḥ ṛṣayaḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ rājānaḥ prathita ojasaḥ brahmā ca viṣṇunā sārdham āhūtaḥ tena dhīmatā devān sarvān ca bhāga artham ahūtān padmasaṃbhavaḥ dṛṣṭvā śivena rahitān dakṣam prati evam abravīt aho dakṣa mahā mūṃḍha durbuddhe kim kṛtam tvayā devāḥ sarve samāhūtāḥ śaṃkareṇa vinā katham antaryāmī sa viśveśaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām bhoktā sa sarva yajñānām śaṃkaraḥ paramārthataḥ ete ca munayaḥ sarve tava sāhāyya kāriṇaḥ na jānanti param bhāvam mahādevasya śūlinaḥ ete ca devāḥ śakra ādyāḥ āgatāḥ yajña bhāginaḥ tad māyā mohitāḥ sarve na jānanti pinākinam yasya pāda rajaḥ sparśāt brahmatvam prāptavān aham dharma adharma vyavasthā ca varṇāḥ ca eva ca tiṣṭhanti śāsanāt tasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ sā ca śaktiḥ parā gaurī sva icchā vigraha cāriṇī kaḥ tām jānāti viśveśīm īśvara ardha śarīriṇīm aham na adya api jānāmi cakrī śakrasya kā kathā sva icchā vigraha rūpiṇyā gauryā saha pinākadhṛt bhrāmayati akhilam viśvam iti satyam na saṃśayaḥ saḥ eva badhnāti paśūn asmad ādīn maheśvaraḥ saḥ eva mocakaḥ devaḥ paśūnām naḥ iti śrutiḥ nāma saṃkīrtanāt yasya bhidyate pāpañjaram śaṃbhoḥ avajñā sthātavyam na eva sūribhiḥ sūtaḥ uvāca dadhīciḥ abravīt akṣam munīnām agraṇīḥ svayam dadhīciḥ uvāca katham deva adhideva īśaḥ karma sākṣī sanātanaḥ viśveśvaraḥ mahādevaḥ tvayā dakṣa na pūjyate vācakaḥ praṇavaḥ yasya jñāna mūrteḥ umāpateḥ anugraham vinā tasya katham jānāti śūlinam prasaṅgāt kautukāt lobhāt bhayāt ajñānataḥ api vā aho dakṣa tava ajñānam tava nāśasya kāraṇam evam dadhīceḥ vacanam śrutvā dakṣaḥ vicakṣaṇaḥ dadhīcim abravīt viprāḥ śakra ādīnām ca saṃnidhau dakṣaḥ uvāca na aham nārāyaṇāt devāt paśyāmi anyam dvijottama kāraṇam sarva vastūnām su niścitam dadhīciḥ uvāca saḥ eva kāraṇam na anyaḥ viṣṇoḥ api hi vai śrutiḥ yajñasya pālakaḥ viṣṇuḥ iti yat niścitam tvayā bhaviṣyati anyathā eva āśu paśyataḥ kamalāpateḥ ete ca brāhmaṇāḥ sarve ye dviṣā enti maheśvaram pāpaṇḍa ācāra niratāḥ sarve niraya gāminaḥ kalau yuge tu saṃprāpte daridrāḥ śūdra yājakāḥ sarvasmāt adhikaḥ rudraḥ paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ tu yuṣmākam mā dijyā karī gatiḥ sva āśramam munibhiḥ juṣṭam oṃkāram narmadā taṭe dakṣa yajñasya vṛttāntam śrutvā devaṛṣeḥ mukhāt mā āha viśva adhikam rudram mãṇat ārti prabhañjanam nirīkṣyamāṇam deveśī parānanda eka vigraham śrī devī uvāca yaḥ ayam prācetasaḥ dakṣaḥ pitā me pūrva janmani āvām avajñāya katham yajñam kartum pracakrame devāḥ sarve samāhūtāḥ viṣṇunā saha śaṃkara ādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ sādhyāḥ ca eva ṛṣayaḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ daiteyāḥ dānavāḥ ca ye rājānaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāḥ tathā avajñā kāriṇaḥ tasya yajñam śīghram vināśaya evam devyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā devadevaḥ pinākadhṛt asṛjat tad kṣaṇāt śaṃbhu vīrabhadram mahā balam sahasra bāhum jaṭilam duṣṭānām ca bhayaṃkaram bhaktānām vara dam devam sūrya soma agni locanam umā kopa udbhavā devī bhadrakālī bhayaṃkarī anyāḥ ca devyaḥ rudrāḥ ca śataśas roma saṃbhavaḥ bhadrakālyā saha tadā vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ gatvā sa yajñam dakṣasya bhasmasāt akarot vijāḥ dakṣaḥ tat adbhutam karma dṛṣṭvā atha bhaya vihvalaḥ gataḥ tat śaraṇam śīghram vīrabhadrasya śūlinaḥ uvāca vīrabhadraḥ tam dakṣam prācetasam dvijāḥ tasya pāpa vimokṣāya kāruṇya amṛta vāridhiḥ gaccha vārāṇasīm dakṣa sarva pāpa praṇāśinīm anugraha artham lokānām yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ anena eva śarīreṇa tatra mokṣam gamiṣyasi sūtaḥ uvāca vīrabhadrasya vacanam śrutvā dakṣaḥ mahāmatiḥ gatvā vārāṇasīm śīghram sarva saṅga vivarjitaḥ pratiṣṭhāpya mahā liṅga gaṅgā tīre manorame ārādhya parayā bhaktyā tasmāt liṅge layam gataḥ dakṣeśvarasya māhātmyam kathitam muni puṅgavāḥ trilocanasya māhātmyam sāṃpratam varṇyate mayā iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde dakṣeśvaramāhātmyādikathanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca trilocanāt param liṅgam vārāṇasyām na dṛśyate yāni sthitāni liṅgāni vārāṇasyām dvijottamāḥ dṛṣṭāni eva bhavanti eva dṛṣṭe liṅga trilocane asaṃkhyātāni pāpāni jñānataḥ ajñānataḥ api vā kṛtāni nāśayati evam devadevaḥ trilocanaḥ māyā pāśena baddhānām sarveṣām prāṇinām api paścima abhimukham liṅgam sarpa mekhala maṇḍitam tasya darśana mātreṇa koṭi liṅga arcanam phalam trilocanam su saṃpūjya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ yayau kāmeśvaram draṣṭum siddha liṅgam anuttamam prasannaḥ vividhāḥ siddhīḥ sarveṣām api durlabhāḥ kṛtānām kriyamāṇānām sarveṣām tapasām api tasya dakṣiṇa digbhāge kāmakuṇḍam iti smṛtam tatra snātvā naraḥ bhaktyā dṛṣṭvā kāmeśvaram śivam anyāni api ca liṅgāni vārāṇasyām sthitāni api saṃkhyām api na jānāti teṣām deva vaturmukhaḥ kaḥ vā vadati māhātmyam ṛte devāt maheśvarāt nandīśvaraḥ vā jānāti prasādāgirijā pateḥ atha satyavatī sūnu draṣṭum devīm śivām parām viśāla akṣī dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ yatra saṃnihitā śivā tām dṛṣṭvā vidhivat bhaktyā saṃpūjya ca mahā muniḥ parīnanda ātmikām gaurīm stutim matvā cakāra saḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca viśāla akṣi namaḥ tubhyam para brahma ātmake śive tvam eva mātā sarveṣām brahma ādīnām divaukasām ṛjvī kuṇḍalinī sukṣmā yoga siddhi pradāyinī svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā meghāḥ lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā sarva śakti mayī śivā aparṇā ca ekaparṇā ca tathā ca ekaikapāṭalā umā haimavatī ca api kalyāṇī caitra mātṛkā khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurī iti viśrutā gaṇa ambikā mahā devī nandinī jātavedasī sāvitrī vara dā puṇyā pāvanī loka viśrutā āryatī niyatī raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī gautamī kauśikī ca assrthā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī vṛṣadhvajā śūladharā paramā brahmacāriṇī mahendra upendra mātā ca pārvatī siṃhavāhanā evam stutvā viśāla akṣī divyaiḥ taiḥ su nāmabhiḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ abhavat vyāsaḥ vārāṇasyām dvijottamāḥ yaḥ paśyati viśāla akṣīm snātvā gaṅgā ambhasi dvijāḥ vārāṇasyāḥ tu māhātmyam iti kiṃcid mayā uditam yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api yāti māheśvaram padam iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde trilocana māhātmya ādi kathanam namāmaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kim lakṣaṇam purāṇānām teṣām dānena kim phalam anyeṣām api dānānām vratānām ca viśeṣataḥ varṇānām āśramāṇām ca teṣām vai lakṣaṇam yathā tatas śrāddha vidhānam ca prāyaścittam katham bhavet mātsyam ca gāruḍam proktam brahmāṇḍam ca tatas param bhāga dvayena kathitam brahmāṇḍam ati saṃjñitam khilāni upapurāṇāni yāni ca uktāni sūribhiḥ saṃhitā dvaya saṃyuktam puṇyam śiva kathā āśrayam āyā sanatkumāra uktā dvitīyā sūrya bhāṣitā iyam puṇyatamā khyātā saṃhitā pāpa nāśinī dānam asya purāṇasya dānānām uttamam dvijāḥ yāni dānāni lokeṣu prasiddhāni dvijottamāḥ sarveṣām phalam āpnoti caturdaśyām na saṃśayaḥ brāhmam purāṇam prathamam dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ vaiṣṇavam viṣṇum uddiśya dvādaśyām prayataḥ śuciḥ anūcānāya yaḥ dadyāt vaiṣṇavam padam āpnuyāt dadāti sūrya bhaktāya yaḥ tu bhāgavatam dvijāḥ vaiśākhe śukla pakṣasya tṛtīyā akṣaya saṃjñitā tasyām tithau saṃyata ātmā brāhmaṇāya āhita āśaye bhaviṣya ākhyam purāṇam tu dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ ma.rkaṇḍeyam tu yaḥ dadyāt saptabhyām prayata ātmavān rājasūya sva yajñasya phalam bhavati śāśvatam dadāti nāradīyam yaḥ caturdaśyām samāhitaḥ kārtikasya caturdaśyām śukla pakṣasya suvaitāḥ laiṅgam dadyāt vijendrāya śiva arcana ratāya vai dvādaśyām saṃyataḥ bhūtvā brāhmaṇāya tapasvine yaḥ vai dadāti vārāham viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati skāndam śivacaturdaśyām pradadyāt śvi yogine jñānī bhavati vipra indrāḥ mahādeva prasādataḥ dvādaśyām vā caturdaśyām dadyāt vāmanam uttamam mātsyam dadyāt dvijendrāya prayati ittarāyaṇe gāruḍam śivam uddiśya dadyāt śvi tithau dvijāḥ śivasya puratas bhaktyā saṃprāpte dakṣiṇāyane gaṇa ādhipatyam ānoti devadevasya śūlinaḥ evam uktaḥ purāṇānām kramaḥ dānena yat phalam iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde brāhmādipurāṇakramadānaphalakathanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca dānam pātre pradātavyam na apātre api aṇu mātrakam pātra bhūtān pravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṅgavāḥ dānena māpnuyāt saukhyam rūpam kānti yaśaḥ balam dānena śatrūn jayati vyādhiḥ dānena naśyati taram ādānāya sat pātram vicārya eva prayatnataḥ veda vedāṅga tatva jñāḥ śāntāḥ ca eva jita indriyāḥ śrauta smārta kriyā niṣṭhāḥ satya niṣṭhāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ tapasvi nara tīrthatāḥ kṛtajñāḥ mita bhāṣiṇaḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇaiḥ atāḥ svādhyāya śīlinaḥ mahādeva arcana ratāḥ bhūtiśāsana bhūṣitāḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ sūrya bhaktāḥ vā pātra bhūtāḥ dvijottamāḥ uttamaḥ sarva pātrāṇām taramaiḥ dattam tat akṣayam tasmāt pāyatamam jñātvā śiva bhaktam akalmaṣam dānam pāpa viśuddhaya artham śraddhayā yat pradīyate proktam naimittikam dānam ṛṣibhiḥ veda vādibhiḥ putra artham vā dhana artha vā svarga artham vā anyatas api vā dānam tat vimalam proktam kevalam mokṣa sādhanam yat kiṃcid īyate dānam daridrāya viśeṣataḥ su alpām api mahīm yaḥ tu dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ sa yāti brahma sadanam yatra devaḥ svayam virāj ikṣu godhūma tuvarī yavaiḥ ca sahitām mahīm api gocarma mātrām yaḥ dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ śiva bhaktāya śāntāya sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate na bhūmi dānāt adhikam dānam asti iha bhū tale hi daridrāya dattam bhavati ca akṣayam āḍhayāya nā eva dātavyam bhūmi dānam viśeṣataḥ yaiḥ dattāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca grāmāḥ parama dhārmikaiḥ gṛhṇanti ye karam teṣu lobha andhāḥ pāpinaḥ nṛpāḥ tad ante makṣikāḥ yūkāḥ matkuṇāḥ maśakāḥ tathā kṛmayaḥ jālapāda arthe śūkarāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ tathā śvānaḥ godhāḥ śaśāḥ sedhāḥ gardabha aśva pipīlikāḥ mūṣakāḥ kṛkalāsāḥ ca vṛkṣa gulma ādayaḥ tathā na teṣām niṣkṛtiḥ ddaṣṭā prāyaścitta śataiḥ api brahma hā śuddhim ānoti kālena muni puṅgavāḥ dvija grāma kara grāhī na eva śuddhim avāpnuyāt vimaidāna kara ādānāt adhikam nā asti pātakam dānānām uttamam dānam vidyā dānam viduḥ budhāḥ tat ca dānam vinītāya varṇa āśrama ratāya ca brāhmaṇāya eva śāntāya śuśrūṣaṇa ratāya ca anna dānam praśaṃsanti viduṣaḥ veda vādinaḥ yatas prāṇāḥ prāṇa dāna samam hi tat a parīkṣya eva sarvebhyaḥ iti svāyaṃbhu śāsanāt mītaḥ ca bhagavān ranena eva śacīpatiḥ tasmāt viśiṣṭam tadā iyam āhuḥ veda vidaḥ budhāḥ na adhvagāya niṣiddham tat iti devaḥ abravīt raviḥ jīvanam sarva bhūtānām jalam eva dvijottamāḥ tiladaḥ putram āproti vāsaḥ daḥ kāntim uttamām dīpadī nirmalām dṛṣṭim yāna daḥ śriyam uttamām śayyā pradaḥ śvā api tathā dhānya daḥ saukhyam uttamam tena dānena mahatā sāyujyam brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam gṛhītvā vetanam vedam yaḥ adhyāpayati mūḍha dhīḥ adhīte yaḥ hi vā dattvā tau ubhau pāpinī smṛtau surā bhāṇḍa gatam toyam yathā bhavati ninditam gavām grāsa pradānena mucyate sarva pātakaiḥ yāni bhojyāni mūlāni phalāni vividhāni ca śākāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca dattvā atyantam sukhī bhavet indhanānām pradānena jāṭhara agni pradīpanam roga hīnaḥ sa dīrgha āyuḥ sukhī bhavati sarvadā gām alaṃkṛtya yaḥ dadyāt sa vatsām ca sa dakṣiṇām ṣoḍaśa ṛtavaḥ ye ca dānam tīrtheṣu yat smṛtam tat akṣayam bhavet dānam yogine ca viśeṣataḥ saṃkrānti ādiṣu kāleṣu dattam bhavati ca akṣayam śivam uddiśya yat dattam su alpam vā yadi vā bahu śivālaye viśeṣeṇa dattam bhavati ca akṣayam viśākha ṛkṣeṇa saṃyuktā vaiśākhī pūrṇimā bhavet tasyām tithau tu saṃpūjya brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā kṛṣṇaiḥ eva tilaiḥ vidvān madhuna vā api upoṣitaḥ dharmarājaḥ yamaḥ sākṣāt mīyatām iti śaktitaḥ yāvajjīvam kṛtaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiḥ vā manogataiḥ mucyate tad kṣaṇāt eva dharmarāja prasādataḥ kṛṣṇājine tilān kṛtvā hiraṇyam madhu sarpiṣī gām annam uda kumbham ca vaiśākhyām saṃprayacchati yā śiva tithiḥ mādhe kṛṣṇa caturdaśī dadāti hema vāsaḥ vā phalam dhānyam atha api vā abhayam sarva bhūtebhyaḥ dadyāt dānam param smṛtam paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt vā api go dānasya phalam labhet iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī sore sūta śonaka saṃvāde dānāha vimādikathanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca anyat vratam idam vakṣye śṛṇudhvam sunieṅgavāḥ śivena kathitam sākṣāt svayam skandāya pṛcchate devadeva mahādeva śaśāṅka kṛta śekhara bharga viśveśvara īśāna kāruṇya amṛta vāridhe kasya prasīdati kṣipram kena vā jñāyate bhavān yogaḥ tvad viṣayaḥ kaḥ vā jñānam tvad vipayam ca īśvaraḥ uvāca sarva āśī sarva bhakṣī vā sarva ācāra vilopakaḥ mad paraḥ vāmanaḥ kāyaiḥ muktaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ tuṣṭaḥ aham bhakti leśena kṣipram yacche param padam tripuṇḍra dhārī satatam śāntaḥ rudra akṣa kaṅkaṇaḥ sūrya vahni indu bhaktānām uttamaḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ paraḥ vaiṣṇavānām sahastrebhyaḥ śiva bhaktaḥ viśiṣyate yadi pāpa rataḥ krūraḥ sva āśrama ācāra varjitaḥ sam ye api dambham samāśritya bhaktānām upajīvikāḥ saṃsārāt te api mucyante kim punar mad parāḥ janāḥ mad bhaktānām ca māhātmyam kaḥ vā jānāti tattvāt ajāne aham tvam ca jānāsi nandī jānāti vā guha mārga sthaḥ vā api amārga sthaḥ mūrkhaḥ vā praṇḍitaḥ api vā sa vaḥ smin pustake caturdaśa adhyāya sthāne saṃgṛhītaḥ advaitam ekam parasam ātmānam jñāna vigraham paśyanti jñāninaḥ tu ekam ātma rūpam idam jagat aham ātmā vibhuḥ śuddhaḥ sphaṭika upala saṃnibhaḥ upādhi rahitaḥ śāntaḥ svayam jyotiḥ prakāśakaḥ ātmani eva akhilam bhāti śuktikā rajatam yathā śukti tattva parijñānāt tad nāśaḥ tadvat ātmani na tena lipyate hi ātmā puṇya apuṇya ākhya karmaṇā buddhi ādayaḥ guṇāḥ sarve bhūt buddheḥ akṛtiḥ ahaṃkārāt ca sūkṣmāṇi tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca sūkṣmebhyaḥ pañca bhūtāni tebhyaḥ sthūlam idam jagat caturviṃśakam avyaktam puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ na tasya kārya karaṇam kriyā rūpam ca vidyate sva ajñānāt kathitam sarvam ātmani eva iti ca śrutiḥ iti mad viṣayam jñānam kathitam tava putraka iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde śivabhaktamahimādikathanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca sādhanāni aṣṭadhā tasya pravakṣyāmi adhunā śṛṇu yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ tāvat āsanāni api ṣaṣ mukham prāṇāyāmaḥ tatas proktaḥ pratyāhāraḥ ca dhāraṇā dhyānam tathā samādhiḥ ca yoga aṅgāni pracakṣate māḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktāḥ niyamān śṛṇu putraka svādhyāya saṃtoṣaḥ śaucam īśvara pūjanam sarveṣām eva bhūtānām akleśa jananam hi yat satyam asteyam adhunā śṛṇu vauryeṇa vā balena api para sva haraṇam ca yam vyāṇām api anādānam āpadi api yathā icchayā vāndrāyaṇa ādinā yat tu śarīrasya ca śoṣaṇam uttapaḥ kathitam putra svādhyāyam adhunā śṛṇu raṇavaḥ śatarudrīyam tathā atharvaśiraḥ śikhā eteṣām yaḥ japaḥ putra svādhyāyaḥ iti kīrtitaḥ padṛcchā lābha saṃtuṣṭaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ iti paṭhyate bāhye ca abhyantare ca api śuddhiḥ śaucam vidhīyate stuti smaraṇa pūjābhiḥ vāc manaḥ kāya karmabhiḥ mayi bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā putra etat īśvara pūjanam yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ proktāḥ saṃkṣepāt na tu vistarāt daṇḍa tākṣya āsanam śūlam kharga mudgaram eva ca makaram tri patham kāṣṭham sthāṇuḥ vā hasti karṇikam bhīmam vīrāsanam ca api vārāham mṛga vaiṇikam iti etāni āsanāni atra saptaviṃśati saṃkhyayā dvitīyaḥ sajayaḥ proktaḥ dhruvam vyāhṛtimātṛbhiḥ recakaḥ śūnyakaḥ ca eva pūrakaḥ kumbhakaḥ tathā evam caturvidhaḥ bhedaḥ prāṇāyāme atra sūribhiḥ asūnām nāḍayaḥ proktāḥ gama āgama laya āśrayāḥ recanācakaḥ proktaḥ śūnyakaḥ tu yathā sthitaḥ pūrakaḥ pūraṇāt vāyoḥ tad nirodhāt ca kumbhakaḥ dehinaḥ dakṣiṇe bhāge piṅgalā nāḍikā ramṛtā dakṣiṇetara gā yā ca iḍā sā nāḍikā smṛtā padma mūtra nibhā nāḍī kārya ākhyā brahma daivatam tatas śūnyam nirālambam madhye sva ātmani yojayet vāhya sthāt bodhanāt vāyoḥ śūnyaka tvam vinirdiśet āpyāyanam bhavet tena plāvanam kalmaṣasya tu aṅguṣṭha agrāt samārabhya brahmarandhreṇa mocayet saṃkocya kucikā cakram ūrdhvam nītvā rasā trayam saṃkṣobhya śaṅkhinīm samyak tatas brahmaguhām nayet anena śodhayet mārgam aiśvaram vimalam muniḥ sumukṣūṇām sadā vatsa yoga aṅgam yoga siddhaye vihāya vahni mārga tu aṅgulyāḥ tu śanais śanais saumyena ākarṣayet vāyum nābhau ākṛṣya dhārayet jāyate vatsarāt yogī jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ vāyum ākarṣayet vāhyam vāmayā ca udaram bharet nābhi nāsā antarā dhyāyan tris prāṇān ca jayet dhruvam triṣu sthāneṣu dhāraṇāt aṅguṣṭha nābhi nāsā agre vāyum yogī jita āsanaḥ apānam kaṭi deśe tu pṛṣṭhatas vai vinirdiśet nirālambe manaḥ kṛtvā kṣaṇāt prāṇa jitaḥ bhavet indriyāṇām vicaratām viṣayeṣu svabhāvataḥ karmendriyāṇām pañcānām pañcama ādya itara ejane udvātān daśa pañca eva kārayet dhāraṇām budhaḥ prāṇa vāyum nivāya eva manaḥ sūrye antare kṣipet devān ca siddhān gandharva aśva araṇān khecarān gaṇān ṣaṣ māsa abhyāsa yogena sūkṣma jyotiḥ prapaśyati dṛṣṭe na syāt jarā mṛtyuḥ sarvajñaḥ ca prajāyate sphoṭa ākhyā nāḍikā proktā kūrma lokaḥ tadā antare bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca vartamānam ca dūratas jñānam yat tat bhavet nūnam sphoṭa ākhye jñānam abhyaset lalāṭe mūrdhni hṛdaye sadāśivam anusmaret dhyātvā evam ātmani vibhum dhyānam tat sūrayaḥ viduḥ na jighrati na spṛśati na kiṃcid vā samīkṣate guhya udara ādi sthāneṣu vāyum nāsām vicintayet īśaḥ aham iti yogi indraḥ para ānanda eka vigrahaḥ gamana āgamanābhyām yaḥ hīnaḥ vai viṣaya ujjhitaḥ ekāntara unmanībhāvaḥ samādhiḥ abhidhīyate na sthūlam na kṛśam vā api na hrasvam na api lopitam na śuklam na api vā pītam na kṛṣṇam na api karburram kṛtvā hṛd padma nilaye viśva ākhyam viśva saṃbhavam ātmānam sarva bhūtānām parastāt tamasaṃsthitam pradhāna puruṣa atītam ākāśam daharam śivam tad antar sarva bhūtānām īśvaram brahma rūpiṇam dhyāyet anādi madhya antam ānanda ādi guṇa ālayam mahāntam puruṣam brahma brahmāṇam brahma ca avyayam oṃkāra ante saṃsthāpya paramātmani ākāśe devam īśānam dhyāyīta ā ākāśa madhya gam kāraṇam sarva bhāvānām ānanda eka rasa āśrayam purāṇam puruṣam śaṃbhum dhyāyet mucyeta bandhanāt mūḍhaḥ yathā śva lāṅgalaiḥ samudram tartum icchati tathā vinā śaṃbhu sevām saṃsāra taraṇam na hi ānandam brahmaṇaḥ sūkṣmam yat paśyanti mumukṣavaḥ pātum tiṣṭhet maheśena saḥ aśnute yogam aiśvaram na ekalakṣam dvilakṣam vā tri lakṣam na mava ātmakam saṃsthāpya mayi ca ātmānam param jyotiṣi nirguṇe muhūrta tiṣṭhataḥ sākṣātasya ca anubhavaḥ bhavet sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ mad prasādāt bhavet yogī na anyathā krauñcasūdana mām ekam śaraṇam gacchet ajñānam nāśayāmi aham brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca anye ca saṃkarāḥ mad bhakti bhāvanā pūtāḥ yānti mad paramam padam yoginām karmiṇām ca eva tāpasānām yata ātmanām aham eva gatiḥ teṣām na anyat asti iti niśvayaḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure śivara kanda saṃvāde yamaniyamaprāṇāyāmādikathanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhūta kāryayā idam deham āpat roga ākulam param viṣayaḥ pīḍyate deva sukha duḥkha ātmakaiḥ sadā abhibhūtaḥ yadā yogī duḥkhaiḥ adhyātma saṃbhavaiḥ yātanāya upasargāṇām prasādāt yoginām vada īśvaraḥ uvāca sāttvikāḥ rājasāḥ vighnāḥ tāmasāḥ tu iha yoginām prātibhā śravaṇa a vārtā darśana āsvāda vedanāḥ daridraḥ aham aham ca āḍhyaḥ śūraḥ aham durbalaḥ tathā mūrkhaḥ aham ca su vidvān ca surūpaḥ aham arūpavān dātā aham kṛpaṇaḥ ca aham sukhī bhogī aham eva ca akulīnaḥ kulīnaḥ ca kaṇṭakaḥ kaṇṭaka ujjhitaḥ ahaṃkāra mayam kiṃcid yat tat kṛtsnam hi rājasam andha tvam ca eva bādhirya paṅga tvam duṣṭa roga tā śiraḥ rogaḥ jvaraḥ śūla aiyakṣma mūrchā bhrama ādayaḥ rājasāḥ tāmasāḥ sarve tamaḥ uhaṃkāra saṃyutāḥ vyādhayaḥ miśra bhāvena pīḍayanti iha dehinam kevalam jāḍya bhāvena mūḍha tvam mohana tathā ajñāna tvam ca mūka tvam ityādyāḥ tāmasāḥ smṛtāḥ gulakāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca kiṃnara uraga rākṣasāḥ deva dānava raudrāḥ ca daityāḥ mātarajāḥ gaṇāḥ tāmasāḥ tu grahāḥ bhūtāḥ vāyu bhūtāḥ naram sadā pīḍayanti iha vighnāḥ hi yoga abhyāsa ratam grahaiḥ evamādi upasargāṇām vāraṇāya ca dhāraṇām vakṣyāmi vividhām vatsa yoginām siddhi hetave tvak ādi sapta dhātūnām ekībhūtam vicintayet pitta roga abhibhūtaḥ vā yogī yoga parāyaṇaḥ praviśya brahma rūpeṇa deha nirvāṇa jam smaret paittika aśrā upasargāya mānunā timiram yathā nāśayet andha tām yogī divya dṛṣṭiḥ prajāyate pītvā pārthivataśvena su ambham vāyoḥ vināśayet puṣṭiḥ eva atulā tasya sthira svam ruja hīna tā śrotram ākāśa vāyvoḥ ca atra eka tvam vicintayet śṛṇoti dūratas śruta ghārī bhavet sadā viyat mayaḥ atha saṃcārī satata abhyāsa yogataḥ rasanāyām ca tad draṣṭāram sa karṇikam prajñā ca evam smṛtiḥ medhā kavi tvam buddhiḥ uttamā stambhanam duṣṭa tvānām sarva vāyun jayet sadā hṛd saroja gatam devam aṣṭādaśa bhujaiḥ yutam nīla aruṇam mahā kārya kcindra jaṭā dharam siṃha carma ambaram bhīmam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam bhujaṅga mhāra ābharaṇam sarva kaṅka nūpuram jvālā mālā ākulam bhā bhāsita digānanam tayathā vṛṣṭa ma tre tu tasmin nai kṣaṇāt lakṣam ādhāya tatra eva yojayet māye ṣaṇmukha ghṛtam ghṛteṣu eva niyuktam prayāti ca aikyāt aviśeṣa bhāvam iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure śiva skanda saṃvāde sāttvikarājasavighnādikathanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca bavāni saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṅgavāḥ tatra kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī puṇyā sarva pāpa praṇāśanī pustakeṣu yaḥ ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ saḥ eva atra saṃgṛhītaḥ kṛṣṇāṣṭamī vratāt na anyat vatam asti vibhūti dam kṛṣṇāṣṭamī tratam kṛtvā brahmā brahmatvam āpnuyāt viṣṇu tvam prāptavān viṣṇuḥ sureśa tvam śacīpatiḥ candraḥ candra tvam āpannaḥ gaṇeśa tvam gaṇādhipaḥ rakandaḥ senāpati tvam ca tathā ca anye gaṇeśvarāḥ kṛtvā ca aiśvaryam āpannāḥ saubhāgyam deva vallabhāḥ vratasya asya prabhāvena lakṣmyāḥ patiḥ abhūt hariḥ yayātiḥ sārvabhauma tvam tathā ca anye nṛpa uttamāḥ ṛṣayaḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ gandharvāṇām ca kanyakāḥ kṛtvā ca eva parām siddhim prāptāḥ ca muni puṅgavāḥ nandīśvareṇa yat proktam nāradāya mahātmane meroḥ yat akṣiṇam śṛṅgam sura asura namaskṛtam tatra nandīśvaram dṛṣṭvā sarvajñam śaṃbhu vallabham upāsyamānam munibhiḥ stūyamānam marut gaṇaiḥ abravīt praṇipatya atha daṇḍa vat nāradaḥ muniḥ nāradaḥ uvāca saubhāgyam kāntim aiśvaryam apatyam ca yaśaḥ tathā śāśvatīm muktimante ca paśu pāśa vimocanīm bhagavan tat vratam brūhi kāruṇyāt śaṃkara bhiyam kṛṣṇa aṣṭamīvratam śreṣṭham asti devaṛṣe śṛṇu gaṇeśa tvam mayā labdham yena cīrṇena nārada māse mārgaśire prāpte kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām jita indriyaḥ aśvattha dantakāṣṭhena kṛtvā vai dantadhāvanam snānam kṛtvā ca vidhivat tarpaṇam ca eva nārada āgatya bhavanam paścāt pūjayet śaṃkaram prabhum go mūtram prāśya vidhivat upavāsī bhavet niśi atirātrasya yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam bhavet pūjayet śam bhunāmānam bhagavantam maheśvaram vājapeya aṣṭaka phalam prāpnoti śraddhayā anvitaḥ māghe vaṭasya kathitam go kṣīram prāśanam smṛtam māheśvaram su saṃpūjya gomedhasya aṣṭakam phalam phālgune ca tat eva uktam kāryam vai prāśanam ca tat saṃpūjayet mahādevam rājasūya aṣṭakam phalam kāṣṭham audumbaram caitre prāśane varjitāḥ janāḥ śivam saṃpūjya vaiśākhe pītvā ca eva kuśa udakam nara medhā aṣṭa phalam prāpnoti eva hi nārada jyeṣṭhe lākṣam bhavet kāṣṭham pūjyaḥ paśupatiḥ vibhuḥ gavām śṛṅgodakam prāśya svapet evasya saṃnidhau gavām koṭi pradānasya yat puṇyam tat avāpnuyāt āṣāḍhe ca ugranāmānam iṣṭvā prāśya ca gomayam sautrāmaṇyāḥ tu yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam bhavet pālāśam śrāvaṇe proktam śarteṃ saṃpūjya nārada prāśayitvā arka patrāṇi kalpam śiva pure vaset māse bhādrapade aṣṭamyām tryambakam saṃprapūjayet mā aśanam bilva patrasya sarva dīkṣā phalam bhavet āśvine jambu vṛkṣasya dantakāṣṭham udīritam īśvaram pūjayet bhaktyā prāśayet taṇḍula udakam pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam labhet māse tu kārtike aṣṭamyām īśāna ākhyam prapūjayet pañcagavyam sakṛt pītvā agniṣṭoma phalam labhet varṣa ante bhojayet viprāḥ śiva bhakti parāyaṇān śaktyā hiraṇyam vāsāṃsi bhaktyā tebhyaḥ nivedayet sa ratnām tāmra kalaśīm gām alaṃkṛtya nārada alaṃkāram ca vastram ca dakṣiṇām ca sva śaktitaḥ kalpa koṭi śatam sāgram śiva loke mahīyate kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī vratam samyak prāptam devaṛṣe mayā sūtaḥ uvāca evam nandīśvarāt śrutvā nāradaḥ muni puṅgavāḥ kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī vratam puṇyam yayau badarikāśramam vratasya asya prabhāvam yaḥ paṭhet vā śṛṇuyāt api iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvratam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca yat uktam bhānunā yājñavalkyāya yogine yājñavalkyaḥ uvāca jayā ca vijayā ca eva kiṃphalā kiparāyaṇā tasyām viśiṣṭam yat puṇyam vada kaśyapa nandana sūryaḥ uvāca dvādaśī viṣṇu dayitā dvādaśī vaiṣṇavī tithiḥ śuklapakṣe dvijaśreṣṭha vijayā sā prakīrtitā upoṣyā sā prayatnena sarva pāpa praṇāśanī yā tu puṣyeṇa saṃyuktā phālgunasya sitā tu vai sā jayā dvādaśī nāma sarva pāpa kṣayaṃkarī tasyām snātaḥ sadā snātaḥ bhavet vai na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃpūjya vastra puṣpa ādyaiḥ phalam sāyam samaśnute ṛcam ekām adhīte yaḥ śraddhā samanvitaḥ sapta janma kṛtam pāpam su alpam vā yadi vā bahu kurute tasyām snātaḥ dvijottama yaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśīm imām kṣapayet bhaktimān naraḥ ekādaśyām nirāhāraḥ dvādaśyām viṣṇum arcayet pādau prathamam kūrmāya ca tathā kaṭim varāhāya iti jaṭharam narasiṃhāya vai uraḥ vāmanāya iti vai kaṇṭham bhujam rāma dvaya iti ca kṛṣṇa nāmnā ca netre dve buddha nāmnā tathā śiraḥ bhaktyā ca āssrādhya govindam gopālam ca tathā niśi tatas tasya agratas śuddham nyaset kṛṣṇājinam budhaḥ tasya upari tilānām tu kṛṣṇānām āḍhakam nyaset tila alābhe yavāḥ kāryāḥ godhūma āra tad alābhataḥ raupyam tāmram vā pātram kuryāt sva śaktitaḥ pracchādya pātram vāsobhiḥ ahataiḥ su parīkṣitaiḥ sauvarṇa vāmanam kṛtvā sākṣasūtra kamaṇḍalum yathāśaktyā kṛtam haravam kṛta yajña upavītinam evaṃrūpam tu tam kṛtvā vāmanam bhaktimān naraḥ matsyaḥ kūrmaḥ varāhaḥ ca nārasiṃhaḥ atha vāmanaḥ rāmaḥ rāmaḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ ca buddhaḥ kalkī ca te daśa bhaktasya atra viśeṣeṇa phalam koṭi guṇa uttaram chatram ca eva akṣa sūtram ca pāduke guḍikām tathā jāgaram tatra kurvīta gīta vādi nāditaiḥ pradeyam śāstra viduṣe brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine viṣṇu bhaktāya śāntāya viśeṣeṇa dīyate veda adhyetre samam dānam dviguṇam tad vide tathā ācārye dānam ekam ca sahastra guṇitam tathā evam dattvā vidhānena brāhmaṇāya ca bhaktitaḥ mantreṇa anena dātavyam purāṇa paṭhitena ca mantreṇa pratigṛhṇīyāt brāhmaṇaḥ ca dvijottama vāmanaḥ asya pradātā vai vāmanāya namaḥ namaḥ iti dāna mantraḥ vāmanaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vāmanaḥ vai dadāti ca vāmanaḥ tārakaḥ dvābhyām vāmanāya namaḥ namaḥ annam prajāpatiḥ viṣṇu rudra indra śaśi bhāskarāḥ parjanyaḥ varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ salilam keśavaḥ śivaḥ svaṣṭā yamaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ pāpam haratu me sadā viprāṇām bhojanam dattvā yathāśakti atha dakṣiṇām pṛṣadājyam ca saṃprāśya paścāt bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ bhūyas yathā icchayā rātrau sarvatra eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ brahma loka ādi lokeṣu bhuktvā bhogān anekaśas punar svargāt bhuvam prāpya jāyate mahatām kule saptadvīpā ādhipatyam ca prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ iti idam śṛṇuyāt nityam vimuktaḥ sarva pāpebhyaḥ śravaṇadvādaśī phalāt iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta yājñavalkya saṃvāde śravaṇa dvādaśīvratakathanam nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca anyat vratam idam vakṣye śṛṇudhvam muni puṅgavāḥ saubhāgya vardhanam puṇyam mahāpātaka nāśanam sarva duṣṭa upaśamanam sarva aiśvarya madam śivam yam yam kāmayate kāmam tam tam prāpnoti mānavaḥ purā devena rudreṇa dagdhaḥ kāmaḥ durāsadaḥ upoṣitā tithiḥ tena tena anaṅgatrayodaśī śukla pakṣe trayodaśyām māsi mārgaśire dvijāḥ snānam kṛtvā atha vidhinā sa upavāsaḥ jita indriyaḥ śaṃbhu nānā tilaiḥ hoṃmam kuryāt aṣṭa uttaram śatam anaṅga nāmnā saṃpūjya madhu prāśya svapet niśi daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ yogeśvaram su saṃpūjya pauṣe candanam rājasūyasya yajñasya phailam ānoti mānavaḥ nāṭeśvaram su saṃpūjya māgha māse jita indriyaḥ mauktikam prāśya vipra indrāḥ phalam tasya vadāmi aham saṃpūjya phālgune vīram kaḍūnelam vaiśākhe ca mahā rūpam deveśam ca prapūjayet jātīphalam ca saṃprāśya go sahasra phalam labhet jyeṣṭhe pradyumna nāmānam lavaṅgam prāśayet niśi umā bhartā iti nāmānam āṣāḍhe saṃprapūjayet tila udakam tu saṃprāśya puṇḍarīka phalam labhet pūjayet śrāvaṇe śūlapāṇinam parameśvaram māse bhādrapade vimāḥ sadyojātam prapūjayet agarum prāśayitvā tu sarva yajña phalam labhet māse ca āśvayuje prāpte tridaśādhipatim yajet svarṇa udakam tu saṃprāśya svarṇa koṭi phalam labhet viśveśvaram ca kārtikyām pūjayet bhakti saṃyutaḥ pratimāsam pravakṣyāmi dantakāṣṭhāni vai dvijāḥ mallikā khādiram ca eva lakṣa apāmārga jam tathā mālatyāḥ prathamam tāvat tatas marutrakam tathā karavīram tathā kundam arka patrāṇi suvratāḥ tatas mandāra puṣpāṇi mallikā kusumāni ca durvā aṅkurāṇi deyāni naivedyāni yathākramam odanam kṛsaram śarkarā amodakāḥ tathā kaṃsāram yāvakāḥ tatra tatas sauhālikā bhavet pañcakhādyam param proktam ghṛtapūram anantaram nānā vidhānam naivedyam kārtikyām parikalpayet pūjā nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṅgavāḥ śaṃkarāya namaḥ pādau gauye gulphe śivāya ca śivāyai jānunī pūjya śaṃbhavāya udbhavāya ca kaiṭim manmatha nāśāya madanāyai sureḥ īrśvare nābhi bhavāya saṃpūjya bhavānyai namaḥ iti umām vakṣaḥ deva adhidevāya aparṇāyai namaḥ śivām kaṇṭha bhīma ugra rūpāya girijāyai namaḥ śivām skandham tridaśa vandyāya triśūlinyai namaḥ śivām bāhū dhūrjaya iti uktvā dhūsarāyai namaḥ śivām hastau śūladharāya iti śūlinyai namaḥ iti umām mukham devasya saṃpūjya vāmadeva iti vāstaḥ vāmāyai namaḥ iti uktvā nāsām ca eva kapāline mṛḍānyai namaḥ iti uktvā lalāṭam ca indu dhāriṇe alakāyai namaḥ paścāt rinetrāya namaḥ tathā tryakṣyai saṃpūjayet devīm śiraḥ gaṅgādharāya ca kātyāyanīm tatas pūjya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ keśān saṃpūjya vidhivat keśinyai ca namaḥ namaḥ śukla vastreṇa saṃchādya saṃpūjya vidhivat vijāḥ ācāryāya atha tam dadyāt vitta śāyya vivarjitaḥ kalaśāḥ sa udakāḥ deyāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ brāhmaṇān bhojayet bhaktyā śiva bhakti parāyaṇān evam karoti yaḥ viprāḥ bhaktyā anaṅgatrayodaśīm prāpnoti rājyam saubhāgyam putrān ca cira jīvinaḥ śiva lokam ca saṃprāpya śaṃbhoḥ priyatamaḥ bhavet iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde anaṅgatrayodaśīvratakathanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ yat uktam bhavatā sūta naiṣkalam jñānam uttamam śrutam ca akhilam asmābhiḥ manāṃsi hṛṣitāni naḥ bhaktiḥ ca śāśvate śaṃbhau jātā asmākam hi śāśvatī varṇa āśrama ācāra vidhim idānīm brūhi tattvataḥ sūtaḥ uvāca caturṇām api varṇānām vidhim vakṣyāmi suvratāḥ yat uktam bhānunā pūrve manave parameṣṭhine yena viśveśvaraḥ śaṃbhuḥ karma yoga rataiḥ sadā ārādhyate na ca anyena iti eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ śūdraḥ ucyate varṇāḥ catvāraḥ eva ete trayaḥ ādyāḥ dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ pañcamaḥ na upapadyate sarveṣām āśramāṇām ca vihitam daṇḍadhāraṇam na daṇḍena vinā kaśvid āśramī iti nigadyate brahmacārī bhavet daṇḍī kṛṣṇa ajina dharaiḥ tathā mekhalī ca tathā muṇḍī śikhī vā yadi vā jaṭī bhikṣā āhāreṇa satatam vartanam tasya suvratāḥ agni kārya tathā kuryāt sāyam prātar yathāvidhi snātvā saṃtarpya deva ādīn devatā abhyarcanam tatas abhivādana śīlaḥ syāt vṛddheṣu ca yathākramam ādhyātmikam vaidikam vā tathā laukikam eva vā ādadīta guroḥ yasmāt tam pūrvam abhivādayet asau aham iti brūyāt pratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ na abhivāyāḥ tu vipreṇa kṣatriya ādyāḥ kathaṃcana śiṣṭānām ca gṛhāt nityam bhikṣām āhṛtya suvrataḥ nivedya gurave aśrīyāt vāgyataḥ tad anujñayā bhaikṣeṇa vartanam nityam na eka anna ādī vratī bhavet upavāsa samā bhikṣā proktā vai brahmacāriṇām prāc mukhaḥ anna ādi bhuñjīta sūrya abhimukhaḥ eva vā na abādadak mukhaḥ nityam vidhiḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ bhuñjīta maunī satatam smaret evam sadāśivam sa upānatkaḥ jala sthaḥ vā na uṣṇīṣī ca ācamet budhaḥ prāśnīya atris apaḥ pūrvam brāhmaṇa prayataḥ dvijaḥ saṃvṛttā mūlena mukham ca evam upaspṛśet aṅguṣṭha anāmikābhyām ca saṃspṛśet nayana dvayam aṅguṣṭha tarjanībhyām ca saṃspṛśena asikā puṭe kaniṣṭhā aṅguṣṭha yogena spṛśet śratra yugam dvijaḥ sarvābhiḥ aṅgulībhiḥ ca hṛdayam ca talena vā saṃspṛśet vai śiraḥ tadvat aṅguṣṭhena athavā dvayam divā mūtra purīṣe ca śarvaryāḥ dakṣiṇā mukhaḥ ācchādya parṇaiḥ vasudhām tṛṇaiḥ vā mauna saṃyutaḥ śiraḥ prāhṛtya vipra indrāḥ na anyathā ca kadācana pathi goṣṭhe nadī tīre chāyāyām kūpa saṃnidhau tuṣa aṅgāra kapāleṣu na kṣetre na catuṣpathe na udyāne na śmaśāne ca na paśyan tārakā ādikān na ca eva abhimukhaḥ strīṇām guru brāhmaṇayoḥ gavām śaucam paścāt prakurvīta gandha lepa kṣaya avadhi āntaram manasaḥ śuddhiḥ yathā bhavati tat vijāḥ jita indriyaḥ syāt satatam vaśya ātmā akrodhanaḥ śuciḥ prayuñjīta sadā vācam madhurām hita bhāṣiṇīm dyūtam jana parīvādam strī velī ālambhanam tathā sarva paryuṣitam varṇya kṛtam ca lavaṇam tathā mala apakarṣaṇam snānam śūdra ādyaiḥ abhibhāṣaṇam guroḥ avajñām satatam brahmacārī vivarjayet uda kumbham sumanasaḥ go śakṛt mṛttikī kuśān ācamya saṃyataḥ nityam adhīyīta chudak mukhaḥ upasaṃgṛhya tad pādau vīkṣamāṇaḥ guroḥ mukham sarveṣām eva bhūtānām vedaḥ cakṣuḥ sanātanam vedaḥ śreyaskaraḥ puṃsām na anyaḥ iti abravīt raviḥ an adhītya dvijaḥ yaḥ tu śāstrāṇi su bahūni api śṛṇoti brāhmaṇaḥ na asau narakāṇi prapadyate na āscāra phalam āpnoti yathā śūdraḥ tathā eva saḥ śūdra putraḥ sa vijñeyām na veda phalam aśrute vedam vedau tathā veda vedān ca caturaḥ dvijāḥ adhītya guruve dattvā dakṣiṇām ca bhavet gṛhī rūpa lakṣaṇa saṃyuktām kanyām uddāhayet tatas a mātṛ gotra prabhavām asamāna ārṣa gotra jām mātṛtaḥ pañcamāt ūrdhvam pitṛtaḥ saptamāt tathā roga hīnām surūpiṇīm mātṛtaḥ pañcamāt avapitṛttaḥ saptamāt tathā dhārayet vaiṇavīm yaṣṭim antarvāsaḥ tathā uttaram yajñopavīta dvitayam sa udakam ca kamaṇḍalum chatram ca uṣṇīpam amalam pāduke vā api upāna hau raukme ca kuṇḍale nityam kṛtta keśa nakhaḥ śuciḥ paṣṭa ṣṭamyau pañcadaśīm amāvāsyām caturdaśīm brahmacārī bhavet nityam janma ca viśeṣataḥ ādadīta āvasathya agnim juhuyāt jātavedasam akurvāṇaḥ patati āśu nirayān ati bhīṣaṇān kuryāt rahmāṇi karmāṇi saṃdhyā upāsanam eva ca vaiṣavān buddhi sādṛśyam ācaran vicaret sadā tam ācāram niṣeveta sādhūn vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam yaḥ taiḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ dharmaḥ saṃgataḥ sat ācāraḥ sa vai proktaḥ devadevena śaṃbhunā kurukṣetrāḥ ca matsya arthe pāñcālāḥ śūrasena jāḥ ete deśāḥ puṇya deśāḥ sarve ca anye ca ninditāḥ deśepaveṣu nivaset rāhmaṇaiḥ dharma kāṅkṣibhiḥ aṅga vaṅga kaliṅgān ca saurāṣṭram gurjaram tathā ābhīram kauḍūṇam ca eva drāviḍam dakṣiṇāpatham andham ca māgadham ca eva deśān etān ca varjayet nityam svādhyāya śīlaḥ syāt pañcayajña parāyaṇaḥ sāvitrī jāpya nirataḥ śiva bhakti parāyaṇaḥ śrāddha kṛt dāna nirataḥ kṣamā yuktaḥ dayālukaḥ gṛhasthaḥ tu samākhyātaḥ na gṛheṇa gṛhī bhavet na śarīram vinā devaḥ pūjyate girijāpatiḥ brahmacārī gṛhasthaḥ vā vānaprasthaḥ athavā yatiḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde varṇa āśrama ācāra vidhi kathanam saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca vākyam na anṛtam na ca marma bhid na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni na vedānām ca kutsanam nindakānām maheśasya śuddhiḥ na khalu dṛśyate jalam tṛṇam vā śākam vā mṛdam vā kāṣṭham eva vā prāṇān apaharati eṣa yācakaḥ tasya durmatiḥ grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi deva arcana vidhau dvijaiḥ tṛṇam kāṣṭham phalam puṣpam prakāśam vai haret budhaḥ tila mudrā yava ādīnām muṣṭiḥ yā ādyā yadi sthitaiḥ anṛtāt pāradāryāt ca tathā abhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇāt pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ abhivādyaḥ syāt pūrva abhāve paraḥ paraḥ tripuṇḍra dhārī satatam brāhmaṇaḥ sarva karmasu na mūkhaiḥ saha saṃvāsaḥ patitaiḥ na kadācana paiśunyam śuṣka vairāṇi vivādam varjayet sadā dhayantīm gām para kṣetre na ca ācakṣīta kasyacid tithim pakṣasya na brūyāt nakṣatrāṇi na nirdiśet na pāpam pāpinām brūyāt tathā apāpam apāpinām yāni mithyā abhiśastānām patanti aśrṛṇi rodanāt tāni putrān paśūn ghnanti teṣām mithyā abhiśaṃsinām brahmahatyā surā pānam steyam guru aṅga anna āgamaḥ dṛṣṭam virodhanam vṛddhaiḥ nārita midhyā abhiśaṃsini mānam madam tathā śokam dveṣam ca parivarjayet ravivāre na kurvīta bhṛṣṭa bhairava bhakṣaṇam dhana kāmaḥ janaḥ satyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na kuryāt kasyacid pīḍām sutam śiṣyam ca tāḍayet na nadīṣu nadīm brūyāt parvateṣu ca parvatam śiraḥ abhyaṅga avaśiṣṭena tailena aṅgam na lepayet sarpa śastraiḥ krīḍeta svāni khāni na saṃspṛśet na saṃhatābhyām pāṇibhyām kaṇḍūyet ātmanaḥ śiraḥ na aśuddhaḥ paricarena devān kīrtaye dṛṣīn viśveśvaram umākāntam viśva antaryāmiṇam vibhum na brahma ādyaiḥ samam brūyāt śaktibhiḥ na ca pārvatīm brūyāt yadi samam śaṃbhum brahma viṣṇu ādibhiḥ suraiḥ yaḥ kaścid tamasā āviṣṭaḥ kadācid na eva tam spṛśet tathā devīm ca girijām dvijaiḥ śreyaḥ ṛthibhiḥ sadā para striyam na bhāṣeta na ayājyam yājayet vijāḥ na ca āsskāmet guroḥ chāyām na guroḥ sadā vakṣyamāṇena vidhinā snānam kuryāt samāhitaḥ bhūmim vyāhṛtibhiḥ spṛṣṭrā khanamānam ca āśayā uddhṛtā asi iti saṃgṛhya gandha dvāra iti gomayam apa agham iti apāmārga dūrvā saṃgṛhya durvayā jala tīram samāsādya śucau deśe samāhitaḥ ādityāḥ iti saṃprokṣya kūlam tīrthasya suvrataḥ śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya gāyatryā prokṣayet tatas bhāga dvayam sa tām paścāt ekam dikṣu visarjayet avaśiṣṭena bhāgena mantraiḥ vā ālepayet kramāt akṣībhyām iti mantreṇa mukham ālepayet budhaḥ grīvābhyām iti ca grīvām tathā bhujau śarīram yajñam uktvā atha hṛdayam parilepayet nābhim ānanda nanda iti śiṣṭam mūrdhni vinikṣipet mūrdhānam iti mantreṇa tila dūrvā akṣata ādikam hiraṇyaśṛṅgam iti uktvā tīrtham saṃprārthya buddhimān japet śuddha matiḥ paścāt sūktam ca eva aghamarṣaṇam dvipadām ca japet devīm sarva pāpa praṇāśanīm idam tu vāruṇam snānam mantra snānam atha ucyate tu āgneyam bhasmanā snānam vāyavyam rajasā mavām ārdreṇa vāsasā ca anyat mānasam śiva cintanam svānānām ca eva sarveṣām mānasam snānam uttamam traivarṇikānām sarveṣām gāyatrī paramā gatiḥ yat gāyatryāḥ param tattvam devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ iti jñātvā japet vidvān gāyatryāḥ phalam aśnute yaḥ hi anyathā tu manute gāyatrī śiva rūpiṇīm pādācatvāraḥ gāyatryāḥ vedācatvāraḥ eva te viraści viṣṇuḥ deśāḥ pādānām devatāḥ kramāt evam jñātvā vidhānena gāyatrī vedamātaram japet māheśvaram jyotiḥ nityam eva prakāśate upatiṣṭhet atha ādityam rudra rūpiṇam avyayam pāvamānāni sūktāni brahmayajña prasiddhaye japet samāhitaḥ bhūtvā rudrān ca eva viśeṣataḥ ṣaṣ akṣareṇa mantreṇa māna stokyā tathā eva ca na asti iti uvāca bhagavān devadevaḥ svayam raviḥ na a saṃpūjya mahādevam bhuñjīta brāhmaṇaḥ sadā brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām karmiṇām yoginām api kuryāt pañca mahāyajñān gṛhasthaḥ śraddhayā anvitaḥ pañcayajña parityāgāt āśramaḥ uṃdavahīyate devayajñaḥ bhūtayajñaḥ pitṛyajñaḥ tathā aparaḥ mānuṣaḥ brahmayajñaḥ ca pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ huta śeṣeṇa bhūtebhyaḥ bālam bhūta makham viduḥ nitya śrāddham tad ṛddhim pitṛ yajñam pracakṣate yathāśakti annum udṛtya padadyāt rāhmaṇāya vai atithim pūjayet bhaktyā śiva bhāva samanvitaḥ mad adyāt vratakāram vā bhikṣām ca bhava bhāvataḥ etān kṛtvā eva satatam bhuñjīta āśrama dharmabhiḥ anyathā yaḥ hi bhuṅkte annam pretya śūkara tām vrajet yadi viśveśvare sthāṇī bhaktiḥ ekā eva niścalā iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde dvijadharmakathanam nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca śrāddham darśe atha kartavyam aṣṭakāsu ayana dvaye viṣuve ca vyatīpāte tīrtheṣu ca viśeṣataḥ parīkṣya brāhmaṇān samyak veda vedāṅga pāragān viśeṣāt śiva bhaktān ca rudra jāpya parāyaṇān abhāve śiva bhaktānām sat ācāra ratān dvijān bhojayet śraddhayā śrāddhe śiva buddhayā samāhitaḥ vrata upavāsa niratāḥ somapāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ agnihotra parāḥ śāntāḥ vahcāḥ guru pūjakāḥ triṇāciketāḥ śiṣyāḥ ca trimadhu trisuparṇikāḥ mantra brāhmaṇa vettāraḥ adhyātma śāstra niratāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ paṅkti pāvanāḥ ekam vā bhojayet vimam śiva bhakti parāyaṇam tena pūtāḥ bhavanti eva ye kecid paṅkti dūṣakāḥ vadha bandha upajīvī ca vṛṣalaḥ śūdra yojakāḥ veda vikrayiṇaḥ ca anye kopinaḥ kuṇḍa golakau kāyasthāḥ lamba karṇāḥ ca nityam rāja upasevakāḥ nakṣatra tithi vaktāraḥ bhiṣaj śāstra upajīvinaḥ vyādhinaḥ kāvya kartāraḥ gāyakāḥ ca eva gotriṇaḥ veda nindā ratāḥ ca eva kṛtaghnāḥ piśunāḥ tathā hīna atirikta dehāḥ ca śrāddhe varjyāḥ prayatnataḥ adhvānam kalaham krodham putra bhāryā ādi tāḍanam prakṣālayet tatas pādau arcite maṇḍale śubhe vartulam caitra vaiśyasya śūdrasya abhyukṣaṇam smṛtam paścāt śrāddhasya rakṣā artham tilān ca vikiret tatas viśvedevān atha āhūya viśvedevāsaḥ iti ṛcā śaṃnaḥ devyāḥ jalam kṣiptvā sa pavitre tu bhājane yavān yavaḥ asi iti tathā gandha puṣpam ca nikṣipet madadyāt gandha mālya ādi dhūpam vāsāṃsi śaktitas apasavyam tatas kṛtvā pitṛn āvāhayet tatas uśantaḥ tu ati ca ṛcā āvāhya tad anujñayā japet āyantu naḥ ṛcam tilaḥ asi iti nilān tathā pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asi iti tatas anaukaraṇam matam mahādevasya puratas goṣṭhe vā śraddhayā anvitaḥ piṇḍa nirvapaṇam kṛtvā brāhmaṇān ca eva bhojayet vividham pāyasam dadyāt bhakṣyāṇi su bahūni api lehyam coṣyam tathā kāmapuṣpam eva phalam vinā vividhāni api māṃsāni pitṛṇām prīti pūrvakam dattāni api niṣiddhāni śrāddham na eva akṣayam bhavet na aśnāti yaḥ dvijaḥ māṃsam niyuktaḥ pitṛ karmaṇi dharma śāstram purāṇam ca tathā atharvaśiraḥ tathā rudrān ca pauruṣam sūktam brāhmaṇān śrāvayet tatas bhuñjīran brāhmaṇāḥ sarve vāgyatāḥ ghṛta bhojanāḥ vikiram nikṣipet paścāt śeṣam annam atha abravīt dāt vai dakṣiṇām śaktyā svadhākāram udīrayet dātāraḥ naḥ abhivardhantām vājevāja iti vai ṛcam bhoktā ca śrāddha dara tasyām rajanyām maithunam tyajet adhvagaḥ vyasanī ca eva viśeṣeṇa ha anagnikaḥ āmaśrāddham dvijaḥ kuryāt sadā eva hi śraddhayā tu kṛte śrāddhe bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure mṛta śaunaka saṃvāde śrāddhavidhikathanam nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca atha dharmaḥ vanasthānām ucyate śṛṇuta dvijāḥ śarīram ātmanaḥ dṛṣṭvā palita ayaiḥ ca dūṣitam phala mūla aśanaḥ nityam pañcayajña parāyaṇaḥ atithim pūjayet bhaktyā matvā śarvaḥ iti śrutiḥ aṣṭau grāsān ca bhuñjīta cīra vāsāḥ bhavet jaṭī bhavet triṣavaṇaḥ trāyī nityam svādhyāya tatparaḥ dayām ca sarva bhūteṣu na kuryāt niśi bhojanam varjayet grāma jātāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca yadi gacchet vanī bhāryā prāyaścittī bhavet vijaḥ ādigarbhaḥ bhavet tasyāḥ sa cāṇḍāla samaḥ bhavet sarva bhūta anukampī syāt saṃvibhāna rataḥ sadā parivādam mṛpā vādam nidrā ālasyam vivarjayet śīrṇa parṇa aśanaḥ vā syāt kṛcchra vartayet sadā śiva pūjā rataḥ nityam śiva dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ parām gatim avāpnoti dehānte śāśvatam padam vedānta abhyāsa nirataḥ dāntaḥ śāntaḥ jita indriyaḥ jīrṇa kaupīna vāsāḥ syāt muṇḍaḥ nagnaḥ athavā bhavet tridaṇḍī vā bhavet vidvān iti eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā māna apamānayoḥ eka anna ādī bhavet yaḥ tu kadācid lampaṭaḥ yatiḥ niṣkṛtinā eva tasya asti dharma śāstreṣu sarvathā bhavet triṣavaṇa snāyī bhasma uddhūlita vigrahaḥ anantam nirguṇam śāntam puruṣam prakṛteḥ param kāraṇa sarva jagatām ādhāram sarvatomukham cit rūpam sthāṇum ānandam ajaram vibhum jñānī mokṣam avāpnoti virāṭpada makhe rataḥ iti sarvam aśeṣeṇa cāturāśramyam īritam śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde vānaprasthādidharmakathanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ manvantarāṇi teṣām ca caritam tathā pratisargaḥ punar ca eva yathā bhavati kṛtstra aṃśaḥ brūhi naḥ sūca sakale yathā nyāsāt śrutam tvayā śṛṇudhvam ṛṣayaḥ sarve sva icchā līlām maheśituḥ kṣobhyam viśvam idam tena kṣobhakaḥ bhagavant aśivaḥ sa saṃkoca vikāśābhyām pradhāna tve vyavasthitaḥ kṣobhyamānāt pradhānāt ca puṃsaḥ prādurabhūt vijāḥ yat etat vistṛtam bījam pradhāna puruṣa ātmakam buddhi ādayaḥ viśeṣa antāḥ avyaktāt īśvara icchyā puruṣa dhiṣṭhitāt eva jajñire muni puṃgavāḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tatas jajñe tanmātrāṇi tatas dvijāḥ tatas bhūtāni jātāni preritāni śiva icchayā vaikārikāt ahaṃkārāt sargaḥ vaikārikaḥ bhavet taijasāni indriyāṇi āhuḥ devāḥ vaikārikāḥ daśa vaikārikāt taijesaḥ ca tāmasaḥ bhūtādeḥ abhavat sargaḥ bhūta tanmātra saṃjñitaḥ vikurvāṇaḥ tu bhūtoṃdiḥ śabda mātram sasarja ha ākāśaḥ jāyate tasmāt tasya śabdaḥ guṇaḥ mataḥ pavanaḥ ca vikurvāṇaḥ rūpa mātram sasarja ha tejaḥ śva utpadyate tasmāt rūpam tasya guṇam viduḥ tejaḥ tu eva vikurvāṇam rasa mātram abhūt tatas utpadyante tatas ca āpaḥ rasaḥ tāsām guṇaḥ mataḥ gandhāt ca pṛthivī jātā gandhaḥ tasyāḥ tu vai guṇaḥ śabda mātram yat ākāśam sparśa mātram samādṛṇot dviguṇaḥ procyate vāyuḥ śabda sparśa ātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ tathā eva viyataḥ rūpam śabda sparśaḥ guṇau ubhau tejaḥ tatas syāt triguṇam sa śabda sparśa rūpavat rasa mātram guṇāḥ sarve trayaḥ ādyāḥ samāviśan āpaḥ caturguṇāḥ tena gandha mātram samāviśan tasmāt pañca guṇā bhūmiḥ balā bhūteṣu kathyate puruṣa dhiṣṭhita tvāt ca avyakta anugraheṇa ca mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti te tasmin kāryam ca karaṇam saṃsiddham parameṣṭhinaḥ prākṛte aṇḍe virañciḥ tu kṣetrajñaḥ brahma saṃjñitaḥ ādikartā sa bhūtānām brahmā agre samavartata meruḥ ulbam bhavet tasya jarāyuḥ ca api parvatāḥ garbha udakam samudrāḥ ca tasya āsan parameṣṭhinaḥ tatra abhavat viprāḥ sa deva asura mānuṣam adbhiḥ daśaguṇābhiḥ tu bāhyatas aṇḍam samāhṛtam āpaḥ daśaguṇena eva tejasā bahis āvṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva bāhyatas vāyunā āvṛtam vāyuḥ kham tu bhūtādinā āvṛtam mahatā ca eva bhūtādiḥ avyaktena as svṛtaḥ mahān etaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ aṇḍam saptabhiḥ prākṛtaiḥ vṛtam guṇāḥ kāla vaśāt eva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ guṇa sāmye layaḥ jñeyaḥ vaiṣamye sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate brahmāṇḍam eva vipra indrāḥ brahmaṇaḥ kṣetram ucyate kṣetrajñaḥ ca saḥ eva uktaḥ virañciḥ śva prajāpatiḥ sahasra koṭayaḥ santi brahmāṇḍāḥ tiryak ūrdhva jāḥ ājñayā devadevasya mahādevasya śūlinaḥ brahmāṇḍānām asaṃkhyānām brahma viṣṇu hara ātmanām na karaṇam kārya kriyā vā vidyate dvijāḥ sva icchayā bhagavān īśaḥ krīḍati avijayā saha kathitaḥ prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃkṣepāt muni puṃgavāḥ abuddhi pūrvakaḥ tu eṣa brāhmī sṛṣṭiḥ atha ucyate iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde prākṛtasargakathanam nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ saṃvibhāga ratāḥ krūrāḥ te parigrāhiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ete pañca samākhyātāḥ sargāḥ devena bhānunā mahataḥ prathamaḥ sargaḥ jñātavyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ dvijāḥ tanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ saḥ ucyate iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ caturthaḥ mukhya sargaḥ tu mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tathā ūrdhvaśrotasām ṣaṣṭhaḥ deva sargaḥ tu sa smṛtaḥ tatas arvākśrotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ aṣṭamaḥ bhautikaḥ sargaḥ bhūta ādīnām dvijocamāḥ kaumāraḥ prākṛtāḥ vaikṛtāḥ tu imeṃ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī sore sūta śaunaka saṃvāde vārāhakalpa prākṛtādisargakathanam nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca tatas sasarja bhagavān devaḥ asau ātmanaḥ sutān śaṃbhum sanatkumāram ca pañca etān padmasaṃbhavaḥ na sṛṣṭau dadhire buddhim śiva eka dhyāna tatparāḥ sṛṣṭau teṣu anapekṣeṣu moha āviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ prāṇa ātmakaḥ samudbhūtaḥ lalāṭāt brahmaṇaḥ haraḥ kena api hetunā vimāḥ sūrya koṭi sama prabhaḥ rodayitvā abja janmānam tasmāt rudraḥ iti smṛtaḥ anyāni sapta nāmāni śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ bhavaḥ śarvaḥ tathā īśānaḥ paśūnām patiḥ eva ca bhīma ugraḥ mahādevaḥ iti nāmāni sattamāḥ bhūmiḥ āpaḥ analaḥ vāyu vyoma sūrya candramāḥ aṣṭamī dīkṣitaḥ tatra mūrtiḥ īśasya śūlinaḥ yābhiḥ vyāptam idam viśvam viśvasya asya jagat mayaḥ tena viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ iti nāmnā śivaḥ smṛtaḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti nirdiṣṭaḥ candramauliḥ viraścinā sasarja manasā rudrān ātma tulyān maheśvaraḥ nīlakaṇṭhān trinetrān ca jaṭā mukuṭa maṇḍitān vṛṣadhvajān vīta rāgān jarā maraṇa varjitān sarvajña śata koṭīn tān sarva anugrāhiṇaḥ parān dṛṣṭvā tān vividhān rudrān viraściḥ mā āha śaṃkaram jarā maraṇa nirmuktām īdṛśīm mā sṛjaḥ prajām sṛjasva anyām sureśāna prajām mṛtyu samanvitām brahmāṇam abravīt śaṃbhuḥ na asti me tādṛśī prajā tatas prabhṛti viśvātmā na prāsūta śubhāḥ prajāḥ rudraiḥ ātma samudbhūtaiḥ krīḍā yuktaḥ tadā abhavat sthāṇu vaniścalaḥ yasmāt sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ iti smṛtaḥ jñānam vairāgyam aiśvarya tapaḥ satyam kṣamā dhṛtiḥ draṣṭṛ tvam ātma saṃbodhaḥ vaṣiṣṭhātṛ tvam eva ca avyayāni daśa etāni nityam tiṣṭhanti śaṃkare saḥ eva bhagavān īśaḥ viśveśaḥ nīlalohitaḥ tatas tam āha bhagavān brahmā saṃvīkṣya śaṃkaram evam viśveśvaram śaṃbhum samābhāṣya caturmukhaḥ stotreṇa anena tuṣṭāva śirasi ādhāya ca añjalim namaḥ śivāya devāya namaḥ te brahma rūpiṇe śaktiḥ māheśvarī tubhyam tasmai vāyu ātmane namaḥ sṛjati aśeṣam evā idam yaḥ sva karma anurūpataḥ yaḥ śete śeṣa śayane viśvam āvṛtya māyayā ātma anubhūti yogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ brahmāṇḍam yaḥ akhila ādhāram tasmai śeṣa ātmane namaḥ yaḥ parānte para ānandam pītvā divya eka sākṣiṇam yaḥ antarā sarva bhūtānām niyantā tiṣṭhati īśvaraḥ tam sarvasākṣiṇam devam namaḥ te paramātmane yasya keśeṣu jīmūtāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aṅga saṃdhiṣu yam vinidrāḥ yata śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ sama darśinaḥ jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasyai yoga ātmane namaḥ yasya bhāsā vibhāti idam tat aham tamasaḥ param tattvam sadā nirākāram cit rūpam pārameśvaram yayā saṃtarate māyām yogī saṃkṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ apara antām aparyantām tasmai vidyā ātmane namaḥ yaḥ śete śeṣa śayane viśvam āvṛtya māyayā ātma anubhūti yogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ brahmāṇḍam tasmai śeṣa ātmane namaḥ yaḥ parānte para ānandam pītvā divya eka sākṣiṇam yaḥ antarā sarva bhūtānām niyantā tiṣṭhati īśvaraḥ tam sarvasākṣiṇam devam namaḥ te paramātmane yasya keśeṣu jīmūtāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aṅga saṃdhiṣu yam vinidrāḥ yata śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ sama darśinaḥ jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasmai yoga ātmane namaḥ yasya bhāsā vibhāti idam tat aham tamasaḥ param tattvam sadā nirākāram cit rūpam pārameśvaram yayā saṃtarate māyām yogī saṃkṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ apara antām aparyantām tasmai vidyā ātmane namaḥ evam stutvā mahādevam brahmā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ tasthau gṛṇan brahma sanātanam aiśvaryam brahma sadbhāvam vairāgyam ca dadau haraḥ karābhyām su śubhābhyām ca upaspṛśya maheśvaraḥ vyājahāra mahādevaḥ saḥ anugṛhya pitāmaham tvam idānīm mama ādeśāt sṛjasva vividhāḥ prajāḥ sarga rakṣā laya guṇaiḥ nirguṇaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ sa tvam mama agratas putraḥ sṛṣṭi hetoḥ vinirmitaḥ bhā eva dakṣiṇāt aṅgāt vāma aṅgāt puruṣottamaḥ mama etra hṛdayāt udraḥ saṃjātaḥ kāma rūpa dhṛka brahma viṣṇu hara ākhyānām yaḥ paraḥ parameśvaraḥ tam mahāntam mahādevam brahman jānanti sūrayaḥ evam brahmāṇam ābhāṣya dattvā ca vividhān varān tatas ca pāśa vicchittiḥ śivaḥ eva bhavet tatas iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde harotpattyādikathanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ katham sa bhagavān uḥ sarvasya ādyaḥ api san vibhuḥ sūtaḥ uvāca āsīt ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe vai sacarācare nārāyaṇaḥ mahā yogī śete tasmin tamaḥ maye yoganidrām samāsādya śeṣa ahi śayane dvijāḥ brahmā jagāma tam deśam yatra asstre puruṣottamaḥ samutthāpya ca tam brahmā madhusūdanam māyayā moḍitām brahmā sureśvaram brūhi iti ukte abravīt viṣṇuḥ brahmāṇam tejasām nidhiḥ na jānāsi katham mūḍha mām antaryāmiṇam vibhum sarvasya āyam suraśreṣṭham jānīhi iti abravīt vibhuḥ kaḥ bhavān iti tam prāha brahmā harim atha abravīt aham vai sarva bhūtānām ādyaḥ sarva jagat patiḥ brahmāṇam mām param devam jānīhi puruṣa ṛṣabha carācara ātmakam viśvam mayi tiṣṭhati sarvadā praviṣṭaḥ brahmaṇaḥ deham tatra lokān dadarśa saḥ sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ punar brahmāṇam abravīt carācara ātmakāḥ lokān sa deva asura mānuṣān praviśya bhuvanān sarvān dṛṣṭvā abhūt vismitaḥ vidhiḥ na apaśyat nirgamaiḥ dvāram pihitāni ca catriṇā tam abravīt gadā pāṇiḥ brahmāṇam amita dyutiḥ līlā artham etat sakalam pitāmaha kṛtam mayā na mātsaryāt suraśreṣṭha dvāra rodhaḥ mayā kṛtaḥ tvam eva jagataḥ mānyaḥ sarvasya ādyaḥ pitāmahaḥ tatas svayaṃbhūḥ viśva ādi śvakriṇe varam uttamam tatas tam abravīt viṣṇum na āvābhyām vidyate param tvad mayam mad mayam sarvam ekā mūrtiḥ dvidhā sthitā evam nigaditaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā kim na paśyasi viśveśam svayam jyotiḥ sanātanam gacchāssvābhyām param devam adhikam śaraṇam vidhe evam hareḥ nigaditam śrutvā brahmā tam abravīt āvābhyām adhikaḥ kaścid vidyeta iti mudhā hare bhāṣase nidrayā assu iṣṭaḥ tyaja moham mahāmate viṣṇuḥ uvāca mā evam vidhe yat a jñātvā param bhāvam maheśvare asti iti na anyathā aham te bravīmi kamalāsana mohita ātmā na saṃdehaḥ māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ māyī viśva ātmakaḥ rudraḥ māyā śaktiḥ tu śāṃkarī sadā janānām hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaḥ api yaḥ paraiḥ alakṣyaḥ lakṣayan viśvam adhitiṣṭhati sarvadā ananta śaktiḥ a ekātmā bhagavān adhitiṣṭhati yasya śaṃbhoḥ parā śaktiḥ bhāva gamyā manoharā nirguṇā sva guṇaiḥ eva nigūḍhā niṣkalā śivā ayam ādiḥ anādi antaḥ svabhāvāt eva nirmalaḥ anantaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca sva icchā adhīnaḥ śvara acaraḥ tadīyam trividham rūpam sthūla sūkṣmam tatas param asmad ādyaiḥ suraiḥ dṛśyam sthūlam sūkṣmam tu yogibhiḥ prasādāt eva sā bhaktiḥ prasādaḥ bhakti saṃbhavaḥ yathā iha aṅkurataḥ bījam bījataḥ vā yathā aṅkuraḥ tasya prasāda leśena paśoḥ pāśa parikṣayaḥ tasmāt paśupatiḥ śaṃbhuḥ paśavaḥ tu asmad ādayaḥ sarveṣām mukti daḥ śaṃbhuḥ teṣām bhāva anurūpataḥ vālaḥ vā taruṇaḥ vā atha vṛddhaḥ vā mucyate paraḥ kaścid kṣīṇa paḍhaḥ bhūtvā punar āvartya mucyate tasmāt nā eka prakāreṇa narāṇām muktiḥ iṣyate jñāna bhāva anurūpeṇa prasādena eva nirvṛtiḥ tvam ekā bhagavat mūrtiḥ anyā nārāyaṇī parā raudrī tṛtīyā kathitā jagat saṃhāra kāriṇī etāsām prerakaḥ śaṃbhuḥ svam sve kārye caturmukha nirguṇaḥ api guṇa adhyakṣaḥ svatantra aiśvarya vigrahaḥ tam īśvaram mahādevam na paśyasi katham vidhe divyam dadāmi te cakṣuḥ yena paśyasi tam śivam brahmā labdhvā param jñānam aiśvaram nirguṇam param tam eva śaraṇam gatvā saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ prītaḥ bhūtvā mahādevaḥ caturmukham atha abravīt tvām eva putram icchāmi tvayā vā sadṛśam sutam tvad māyā mohitaḥ śaṃbho na vedmi tvām param śivam namāmi tava pāda abjam yoginām bhava bheṣajam śrutvā viraścaiḥ vacanam devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk brahmāṇam abravīt putram samālokya atha cakriṇam jñānam mad viṣayam kṣipram bhaviṣyati tava anagha eṣa yogi īśvaraḥ śāṅga mama eva aṃśaḥ na saṃśayaḥ sāhāyye bhavitā brahman mama ādeśāt tava anagha evam dattvā varam śaṃbhu brahmaṇe dvijasattamāḥ athā bravīt hṛṣīkeśam prāñjalim puratas sthitam varam varaya dāsyāmi tava nārāyaṇa avyaya jñāna jñeya ātmakam viśvam tvad mayam mad mayam hare jñātā aham jñāna rūpaḥ tvam mantā aham tvam matire prakṛtiḥ tvam suraśreṣṭha puruṣaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ tvam candramāḥ aham sūryaḥ śarvarī tvam aham dinam tvam eva māyā viśvasya māyā aham parama vibho evam śaṃbhoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā vāsudevaḥ nirañjanaḥ abravīt paramātmānam mahādevam dvijottamāḥ viṣṇuḥ uvāca evam astu iti atha ābhāṣya ca śārṅgiṇam pālaya etat mama ādeśāt iti uktvā antarhitaḥ haraḥ tathā sarvam aśeṣeṇa kathitam muni puṃgavāḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde brahma padmayonitvādikathanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ katham bhagavatī gaurī śaṃkara ardha śarīriṇī ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ para brahma ātmikā nityā paramā ākāśa madhya gā sarva śakti mayī śāntā nirguṇā nirupadravā svar bhābhiḥ bhāsayantīm viśvam etat sureśvarī pṛthak śarīram akarot katham sā parameśvarī sūtaḥ uvāca viśveśvarāt mahādevāt varam labdhvā pitāmahaḥ prajāḥ sasarja bhagavān na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ duḥkhitaḥ abhūt tadā brahmā prajāḥ dṛṣṭvā tu durbalāḥ mene akṛtārtham ātmānam prādurbhūtaḥ tatas haraḥ brahmāṇam abravīt śaṃbhuḥ jñātam tvad duḥkha kāraṇam ardhanārīśvaraḥ devaḥ svayam viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ nārī bhāgān mahādevaḥ sasarja pṛthak īśvarīm brahma ātmikām parām śakti koṭi vāla arka bhāsurām kṣetrajña śakti nilaya ūm paramākāśa madhya gām brahma indra viṣṇu namitā ṣṭa mūrti aṅginīm ajām pradhāna puruṣa atītām sāvitrīm vedamātaram ṛk yajuḥ sāma nilayām ṛjvīm kuṇḍalinīm parām viśveśvarīm viśva mayīm viśveśvara prativratām viśva saṃhāra karaṇī viśva māyā pravartinīm sarga sthiti anta kāriṇī vyakta avyakta svarūpiṇīm pāhi mām devadeveśa śaraṇa āgata vatsale tvam mātā mama kalyāṇi pitā sarva īśvaraḥ śivaḥ mṛṣṭaḥ aham tripura ghnena sṛṣṭi artha śaṃkara priye vividha aśva prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ na vṛddhim upayānti tāḥ tatas param prajāḥ sarvāḥ maithuna prabhavāḥ kila saṃvadhātum icchāmi kṛtvā sṛṣṭim atas param śaktīn om khalu sarvāsām tvattaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ na eva sṛṣṭam yat kulam śive sarveṣām dehinām devi sarva śakti pradāyinī mama sṛṣṭi vivṛddhaya artham aṃśena ekena śāśvate mā arthitā vai tadā devī brahmaṇā muni puṃgavāḥ ekām śaktim bhruvoḥ madhyāt sasarja ātma sama prabhām ā tām mahasan prekṣya devīm viśveśvaraḥ haraḥ ādāya śirasā śaṃbhoḥ ājñā sā parameśvarī abhavat dakṣa duhitā kha icchayā brahma rūpiṇī punar ādyā parā śaktiḥ śaṃbho deham samāviśat ardhanārīśvaraḥ devaḥ vibhāti iti hi naḥ śrutiḥ tatas prabhṛti vipra indrāḥ maithuna prabhavāḥ prajāḥ evam vaḥ kathitāḥ vimāḥ devyāḥ saṃbhūtiḥ uttamā paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt vā api saṃtatiḥ tasya vardhate iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde gaurīpṛthaśarīratvādikathanam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca asṛjat bhagavān brahmā kalmaṣān dakṣam atrim vasiṣṭham ca saḥ asajat manasā vibhuḥ deva asura manuṣyān ca pitṛ śāpi prajāpatiḥ asṛjat kramaśas sarvān andhakāre ca rākṣasān gandhaiḥ sa tathā nāgān yakṣān ca api sahasraśas asṛjan pukhataḥ vimān dāhubhyām kṣatriyān viḥ ūru dvayāt tathā vaiśyān pādāt śūdrān sasarja ha chandāṃsi vedān yajñān atha kalpasūtram atas param vedāṅgāni tatas sṛṣṭvā maithuna prabhavām atas sṛṣṭim kartum matim cakre devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ ardhena nārī yā tasmāt śatarūpā abhyajāyata svāyaṃbhuvam manum brahmā ca arthena vapuṣā asṛjat śatarūpā ca yā devī tapaḥ taptvā su duśvaram kanyā catuṣṭayam ca eva śraddhā ādīnām dvijottamāḥ kardamam ca ambarīṣam ca pulahāt suṣuve kṣamā durvāsasam tathā somam dattātreyam ca yoginam sinīvālī kuhūm ca eva rākām anumatim tathā smṛtiśva aṅgirasaḥ putrīḥ sūte lakṣaṇa saṃyutāḥ mītyām pulastyāt abhavat dataḥ nirmānavaiḥ sutaḥ pūrva janmāni yaḥ agastyaḥ khyātaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare putrāṇām ṣaṣṭi sāhasram saṃtatiḥ suṣuve kratoḥ varbhūvuḥ saṃtatau teṣām catvāriṃśat pañca ca pāvaka ādyāḥ traya vā ete catvāriṃśat tathā nava yajñeṣu bhāginaḥ sarve tathā sarve tapasvinaḥ rudra arcana parāḥ sarve tripuṇḍra aṅkita mastakāḥ ayajvānaḥ ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ agniṣvāttāḥ barhiṣadaḥ dvidhā teṣām vyavasthitiḥ menām ca dhāriṇīm tatra yoga mārga rate ubhe menā himavataḥ sūte mainākam krauñcam eva ca mentum dhāriṇī sūte mandaram cāru kandaram dhāriṇī suṣuve velām niyaṃtim ca āyatim tathā sāgarāt suṣuve velā sāmudrīm nāma nāmataḥ prācīnavarhiṣā sā ca daśa putrān ajījanat prācetasaḥ iti khyātāḥ sarve svāyaṃbhuve antare matra śāpāt abhūt putraḥ yeṣām dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ atha idānīm manoḥ putra saṃtatim kathayāmi vaḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde marīcyādisargadakṣakanyāsaṃtatikathanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca uttānapādasya sutaḥ dhruvaḥ nāma mahā manāḥ ārādhya paramam devam nārāyaṇam anāmayam nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ tān niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ dhruvasya putrāḥ catvāraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ dhanyat tathā paraḥ haryaḥ śaṃbhuḥ mahātmānaḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ prathita ojasaḥ chāyā pañca sutān sūte sṛṣṭeḥ dharma parāyaṇaun ripum ripuṃjayam vipram ṣalam katejasam ripoḥ bhāryā tu bṛhatī prasūte cakṣuṣam sutam sūte puṣkariṇī putram cakṣuṣā ākṣuṣam manum tad vaṃśa jāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ tuśiva ādayaḥ khyātaḥ sa pṛthivīpālaḥ yena dugdhā vasuṃdharā vāsudeva arcana rataḥ vāsudeva parāyaṇaḥ mītaḥ tam abravīt viṣṇuḥ pṛthum muni vara uttamāḥ āsthāya paramām bhakti bhagavait vācam āśritaḥ pṛthoḥ bhāryā mahābhāgā kālena suṣuve sutau śikhaṇḍinam havirdhānam suśīlaḥ ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ śvetāśvatara nāmānam śiva dhyāna eka tatparam upāsya labdhavān taramā suśīlaḥ yogam aiśvaram ṛyaḥ ūcuḥ suśīlena katham rājñā prāptam jñānam anuttamam sūtaḥ uvāca yaḥ asau śikhaṇḍinaḥ putraḥ brahmacarya āśrame rataḥ vicāraḥ śreyase tasya kadācid samabhūt vijāḥ apaśyat yogibhiḥ juṣṭam mahādeva kṛta ālayam yatra siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ marīci ādyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān tathā ca anye sura asurāḥ samārādhya mahādevam siddhim prāptāḥ hi anekaśas yatra mandākinī gaṅgā rājate hi agha hāriṇī apaśyat āśramam tasyāḥ tīre yogi indra sevitam dhyāyamānaḥ kṣaṇam tatra sthitaḥ viśveśvaram śivam śvetāśvatara nāmānam atha apaśyat mahā munim mahāpāśupatam śāntam jīrṇa kaupīna vāsasam bhasma uddhūlita sarva aṅgam tripuṇḍra tilaka anvitam abhivandya muneḥ pādau śirasā prāñjaliḥ nṛpaḥ abravīt tam muni śreṣṭham sarva bhūta anukampinam tapāṃsi saphalāni eva jātāni tava darśanāt bhavāmi tatra śiṣyaḥ aham rakṣa saṃsāra jāt bhayāt rājānam muni puṃgavāḥ veda abhyāsa rataḥ śāntaḥ bhaya niṣṭhaḥ jita indriyaḥ saṃnyāsa vidhim āśritya suśīlaḥ muktimān bhavet iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde uttānapāda saṃtatyādi kathanam nāma saviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca tu ayaṃbhuvā samāviṣṭaḥ pūrva dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti rugadī ca sura asurān ṣaṣṭim dakṣaḥ asṛjat kanyāḥ asikayām vai prajāpatiḥ saptaviṃśatim somāya catatraḥ ariṣṭanemine dve ca eva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate dve ca eva aṅgirase tat vadau dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ sādhyā viśvā ca saṃkalpā muhūrtī ca hi arundhatī marutvatī vasuḥ bhānuḥ lambā jāmī iti tāḥ daśa sādhyāḥ babhūvuḥ sādhyāyām viśvāyām viśva devatāḥ saṃkalpāyāntu saṃkalpaḥ muhūrta jāḥ vasoḥ atu vasavaḥ proktāḥ bhānoḥ te bhānavaḥ smṛtāḥ lamdāyām ghoṣanāmānaḥ nāgavīthīḥ tu jāmi jāḥ samākhyātāḥ sarva bhūta hita eṣiṇaḥ āpaḥ nalaḥ ca somavān anilaḥ analaḥ matyūpaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ upāsya labdhavān taramā suśīlaḥ yogam aiśvaram ṛyaḥ ūcuḥ suśīlena katham rājñā prāptam jñānam anuttamam sūtaḥ uvāca yaḥ asau śikhaṇḍinaḥ etraḥ brahmacarya āśrame rataḥ vicāraḥ śreyase tasya kadācid samabhūt vijāḥ apaśyat yogibhiḥ juṣṭam mahādeva kṛta ālayam yatra siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ marīci ādyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān tathā ca anye sura asurāḥ samārādhya mahādevam siddhim prāptāḥ hi anekaśas yatra mandākinī gaṅgā rājate hi agha hāriṇī apaśyat āśramam tasyāḥ tīre yogi indra sevitam dhyāyamānaḥ kṣaṇam tatra sthitaḥ viśveśvaram śivam śvetāśvatara nāmānam atha apaśyat mahā munim mahāpāśupatam śāntam jīrṇa kaupīna vāsasam bhasma uddhūlita sarva aṅge tripuṇḍū tilaka anvitam abhivandya muneḥ pādau śirasā prāñjaliḥ nṛpaḥ abravīt tam muni śreṣṭham sarva bhūta anukampinam tapāṃsi saphalāni eva jātāni tava darśanāt bhavāmi tava śiṣyaḥ aham rakṣa saṃsāra jāt bhayāt rājānam muni gavāḥ veda abhyāsa rataḥ śāntaḥ bhaya niṣṭhaḥ jita indriyaḥ iti śrī brahmaṇā uṣa rāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde uttānapāda saṃtatyādi kathanam nāma saha viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca svayaṃbhuvā samāviṣṭaḥ pūrva dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti rururja ca sura asurān prajāpateḥ aṇasya kanyā ari ditā ṣaṣṭim dakṣaḥ asṛjat kanyāḥ vai prajāpatiḥ saptaviṃśatim somāya catas ariṣṭanemine dve ca eva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate ca eva aṅgirase tat vadau dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ sādhyā viśvā ca saṃkalpā muhūrtā ca hi arundhatī marutvatī vasuḥ bhānuḥ lambā jāmī iti tāḥ daśa sādhyāḥ babhūvuḥ sādhyāyām viśvāyām viśva devatāḥ saṃkalpāyāḥ tu saṃkalpaḥ murta jāḥ vasoḥ tu vasavaḥ proktāḥ bhānoḥ te bhānavaḥ smṛtāḥ lambāyām ghoṣanāmānaḥ nāgavīthīḥ tu jāmi jāḥ vasavarate samākhyātāḥ āpaḥ nalaḥ ca somaḥ ca dhruvaḥ ca eva anilaḥ analaḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ viśvakarmā prabhāsasya dharmasya eṣā tu saṃtatiḥ ariṣṭā surasā proktā svadhā surabhiḥ eva ca ca tathā aṃśuḥ dhātā bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā mitraḥ atha varuṇaḥ aryamā vivasvān savitā pūṣā aṃśumān viṣṇuḥ eva ca tuṣitāḥ nāma te cānuṣasya antare manoḥ ādityāḥ aditeḥ putrāḥ proktāḥ vaivasvate antare putra dvayam ditiḥ sūte kaśyapāt muni puṃgavāt hiraṇyakaśipum tu ekam hiraṇyākṣam anantaram śaka ādyāḥ devatāḥ sarvāḥ tena daityena vādhitāḥ brahmāṇam śaraṇam gatvā procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ surāḥ hiraṇyakena daityena śastrān traiḥ sūditāḥ vayam dārāḥ ca apahṛtāḥ tena vajra ādīni āyudhāni ca trāyasva asmān rbhaya trastān śaraṇam na anyat asti naḥ evam suraiḥ nigaditam śrutvā ca eva pitāmahaḥ devaiḥ saha yayau tūrṇam viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ bādhate sakalān devān munīn nirdhūta kalmaṣān yaḥ tam haniṣyati kṣipram na tam paśyāmi mādhava hantum arhasi tam śīghram devānām kārya siddhaye śrutvā nārāyaṇaḥ vākyam īritam tridivaukasām narasya ardha tanum kṛtvā siṃhasya ardha tanum tathā nṛsiṃha rūpī bhagavān hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pure āvirbabhūva bhagavān devaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ muñcan nādam mahā ghoram asurāṇām bhayaṃkaram hiraṇyakaśipuḥ dṛṣṭvā nṛsiṃham ati bhīpaṇam vadhāya preṣayāmāsa prahāda ādīn mahā asurān saṃhādaḥ hādaḥ eva ca hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥ catvāraḥ prathita ojasaḥ a narasiṃhena te sārdham yuyudhuḥ dānavāḥ tadā prahlādaḥ prāhiṇot rāhmam astram tam narakesarim vaiṣṇava astram anuhādaḥ kaumāram ca tathā aparaḥ prāhiṇot vāde āgneyam ca anye mahā asurāḥ catvāri āryāṇi saṃprāpya bhagavantam nṛkesarim babhūvuḥ tāni bhagnāni yathā vajra āhatāḥ dumaḥ gṛhītvā caturaḥ putrān hastābhyām narakesariḥ cikṣepa gaganāt bhūmau gṛhītvā evam punar punar evam tān vyathitān dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam vinivṛttaḥ aśva saṅgrāmāt prahādaḥ daitya rāj tatas jñātvā tu bhagavat bhāvam nṛsiṃha tyā amita ojasaḥ eṣa nārāyaṇaḥ yogī parama ātmā sanātanaḥ putra uditam an ādṛtya hiraṇyakaśipuḥ punar yuyudhe hariṇā sārdham yāvat varṣa śataṃtryam atha viśvātmakaḥ viṣṇuḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ nakhaiḥ vidārayāmāsa hiraṇyakaśipum tadā iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde surāsurasṛṣṭyādikathanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca hiraṇyākṣam mahā bāhum rājye samabhiyojayat saḥ u api devān raṇe jitvā vai palāyitāḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahādevam tapasā ārādhya ca antakam lebhe putram mahā bāhum sarva amara niṣūdanam hiraṇyākṣa bhayāt devāḥ śārṅgiṇam śaraṇam gatāḥ dṛṣṭvā atha bhagavān devān hiraṇyākṣa vadhāya vai vārāham rūpam āsthāya hiraṇyākṣaḥ
